📗 英语学习手册

从你的课堂笔记整理而来 · 按主题分类 · 点击卡片翻转复习

📖 语法速查
🕐 时态体系总览 核心
⬅ 过去 已经发生的事
一般过去时
结构：did（过去式）
过去完成的动作
📌 I took part in a competition.
过去进行时
结构：was/were + doing
过去某一刻正在做
📌 I was minding my own business.
⏫ 现在 当下正在发生 / 与现在有关
一般现在时
结构：do / does
习惯、爱好、事实
📌 I like jazz.
现在进行时
结构：am/is/are + doing
此刻正在做
📌 I'm living here.
现在完成时
结构：have/has + done
过去发生、影响现在
📌 I've been there.
➡ 将来 还没发生、计划或预测
be going to
结构：am/is/are going to + do
提前计划的将来
📌 I'm going to buy new stationery.
will
结构：will + do
临时决定、预测
📌 I will keep in touch with you.
be doing 表将来
结构：am/is/are + doing
已安排好的将来
📌 Rachel is meeting Diane next Friday.
过去进行时 + when 经典句型：was/were doing + when + 一般过去时 = "正在做……这时突然……"
🎯 现在完成时 have/has + done 完整解析 重点突破
一、核心公式
句型结构例句
肯定句 主语 + have/has + 过去分词 I have visited Milan.
否定句 have/has + not + 过去分词 I haven't been there.
疑问句 Have/Has + 主语 + 过去分词? Have you been to Hong Kong?
have vs has：三单主语（he/she/it/单数人名）→ has；其余（I/you/we/they/复数）→ have
两种形式：① have/has + 实义动词过去分词（普通动作）② have/has + been（be 动词的完成式）
二、核心本质：过去动作 → 留下现在结果/影响
不关心动作具体哪一天发生，只看重两点其一：
① 动作发生在过去，但对当下有影响
② 动作从过去持续到现在
时态例句侧重点
一般过去时 I went there in 2019. 带过去时间，只陈述当年去过，和现在无关
现在完成时 I've been there. 不带过去时间，重点：我现在拥有「去过那里」的经历
三、4大用法
用法1：曾经有过某种经历（最常用）
含义：人生到目前为止做过某事，常搭配 ever / never / before
拆解：I've been there.
I = 主语  |  have = 助动词（现完标志） |  been = be 的过去分词（be → was/were → been） |  there = 地点状语

直译：我到过那里 / 我去过那儿
现在影响：我现在熟悉这个地方，不用给我介绍；我有这段旅行经历
例句翻译
She's been to Australia.🔊她去过澳大利亚。
Have you ever been to Hong Kong?🔊你去过中国香港吗？
固定搭配：have been to + 地点 = 去过某地，现已回来
用法2：过去动作，结果留在当下（有直观影响）
例句翻译现在影响
I have lost my wallet.🔊我钱包丢了。现在没钱，没法付款
We have eaten dinner.🔊我们吃过晚饭了。现在不饿，不用点餐
用法3：动作从过去持续到现在（常搭配 for / since）
例句翻译时间起点
We have lived together for six years.🔊我们同居六年了。2020年开始，持续到现在
I have worked in Shenzhen since March 2019.🔊我2019年3月起就在深圳工作。至今还在
for vs since：for + 一段时间（for 3 years）/ since + 过去时间点（since 2019）
用法4：刚刚完成的动作（搭配 just / already / yet）
例句翻译
I've just finished cooking.🔊我刚做完饭。
We have already tried oysters.🔊我们已经吃过生蚝了。
四、关键时间标志词
ever 曾经 never 从未 before 以前 just 刚刚 already 已经 yet 还（否定/疑问） since + 过去时间 for + 一段时间 so far 到目前为止 in my life 这辈子
五、禁忌：不能搭配具体过去时间
❌ I've been there in 2019.
✅ I was there in 2019.（有明确过去年份，只用一般过去时）
六、have been to vs have gone to 极易混
结构含义人现在在哪例句
have been to + 地点 去过某地 ✅ 已回来 I've been to Milan.
我去过米兰，现在不在那。
have gone to + 地点 去了某地 ❌ 还在当地 She has gone to Hong Kong.
她去中国香港了（现在人在那）。
记忆方法：been = "去过"（已回来）/ gone = "去了"（还没回来）
就像中文"我去过北京"vs"他去了北京"，一个强调经历，一个强调人不在
七、I've been there 完整场景
场景1：
A: Do you know Milan?
B: Yes, I've been there.
🇨🇳 A：你了解米兰吗？ B：了解，我去过那儿。（现完：拥有经历，现在熟悉这座城市）

场景2：
A: Let's travel to Maldives this year.
B: I've been there, maybe we pick another place.
🇨🇳 A：我们今年去马尔代夫吧。 B：我去过了，换个地方吧。（现在结果：不想再去）
🚀 三种将来时结构完整拆解 重点突破
一、be going to 表将来
结构公式
am/is/are + going to + 动词原形 do
be 动词变化：I → am  |  he/she/it/单数 → is  |  you/we/they/复数 → are
核心用法：提前计划好的将来
动作是说话前已经规划、打算好要做的事
拆解：I'm going to buy new stationery.
I'm = I am（be 动词适配主语 I） |  going to = 将来结构标记  |  buy = 动词原形

句意：我打算去买新文具（买文具这个想法之前就想好的）
二、will 表将来
结构公式
will + 动词原形 do
will 无人称变化，所有人称都直接用 will（I will / She will / They will）
核心用法：临时决定 / 对未来预测
不是提前规划，是说话当下临时敲定的安排，或是对未来情况的预判
拆解：I will keep in touch with you.
will = 将来情态标记  |  keep = 动词原形

句意：我会和你保持联系（多是当下分别时临时做出的承诺/决定）
三、be doing（现在进行时表将来）
结构公式
am/is/are + 动词-ing 形式 doing
核心用法：已安排敲定好的近期将来
多用于位移类、会面类动词（meet / leave / come / go 等），日程已经确定、时间地点都安排妥当，近期就会发生
拆解：Rachel is meeting Diane next Friday.
is = be 适配单数主语 Rachel  |  meeting = 动词 -ing 形式  |  next Friday = 将来时间状语

句意：雷切尔下周五要和黛安碰面（会面计划已经敲定，时间、安排都定好了）
三者关键对比速记
结构适用场景Planning 程度例句
be going to 提前想好的计划、有迹象要发生的事 提前规划 I'm going to buy new stationery.🔊
will 当场临时决定、纯未来预测 无提前规划 I will keep in touch with you.🔊
be doing 日程完全敲定、时间固定的近期安排 安排最固化 Rachel is meeting Diane next Friday.🔊
一句话区分：
昨天就想好要买 → be going to  |  此刻才决定的 → will  |  日历上已标好的 → be doing
⚡ be going to vs be doing（表将来）超详细对比 新
一、核心定义
be going to — 场景 1：有明显迹象，马上发生（客观预判）
肉眼能看到征兆，立刻会出现
Look! The boy is going to fall off the tree.
看！男孩马上要从树上摔下来。
Look at the dark clouds. It's going to rain.
看乌云，马上要下雨。
be going to — 场景 2：早已做好计划、打算（主观计划）
提前想好、有准备的安排
I am going to visit the flea market this Sunday.
这周日我打算去逛跳蚤市场（提前想好的计划）。
be doing（现在进行时表将来）
仅限位移类动词：go / come / leave / arrive / fly / travel / move
含义：已经敲定、定好时间的出行安排，日程固定，几乎不会变动
I'm leaving for Sydney next year.
我明年动身去悉尼（机票/行程全部定好）。
She's coming to see me tomorrow.
她明天过来看我（双方约好）。
二、3 大关键区别
区别 1：能用的动词范围
✅ be going to：所有动词
He is going to cook dinner. 他准备做饭。
He is going to fall. 他快要摔倒。
⚠️ be doing：仅出行/位移动词
❌ I'm cooking dinner tomorrow.
（cook 不是位移词，不能用）
✅ I'm going to cook dinner tomorrow.
区别 2：计划确定性
🔒 be doing：100% 敲定
行程完全敲定、有车票/约定，确定性最强
We're flying to Mexico tonight.
机票买好，行程固定
💭 be going to：只是打算
心里打算，不一定落实，可更改
I'm going to fly to Mexico someday.
只是想法，没订票
区别 3：预判即将发生
⛔ 只能用 be going to，绝对不能用 be doing
✅ Look out! The wall is going to collapse.
小心！墙马上要塌了。
❌ Look out! The wall is collapsing.
→ "墙正在塌"，不是预判将来
三、同一句话对比，直观看懂
表达含义关键区别
I'm going to visit my grandma.🔊 我打算去看望奶奶 心里计划，还没定具体时间
I'm visiting my grandma this Saturday.🔊 这周六我要去看望奶奶 约好时间，行程确定
四、will / be going to / be doing 三者极简总结
will do
临时突然决定
单纯猜测
无提前计划
This bag is heavy.
→ I will help you.
be going to do
有征兆马上发生
心里打算
适用所有动词
Look at clouds!
→ It's going to rain.
be doing
固定出行日程
仅位移动词
行程确定
I'm flying to Sydney.
机票已买好
五、超直白 2 条铁律（做题直接套）
铁律 1：动词限制
be doing 表将来
只能用：go / come / leave / arrive / fly / travel / move
❌ visit、cook、buy、fall、study… 一律不能用
be going to do
所有动词都能用，无任何限制
✅ 出行、做饭、逛街、摔倒、下雨，全部可以套
铁律 2：计划的确定程度
be doing（位移动词）be going to do
确定程度 100% 敲定 已买票、约好时间、板上钉钉 只是打算 心里想法，没落实票据/约定
例句 I'm leaving for Sydney next year.
机票租房全部搞定🔊		 I'm going to leave for Sydney someday.
只是想法，没订票🔊
六、两种绝对不能互换的场景
场景 1：预判马上发生（危险/天气）→ 只能用 be going to
✅ Look! He's going to fall off the tree.
看！他马上要从树上摔下来。
❌ Look! He's falling off the tree.
→ "他正在往下摔"（已经摔了，不是预判将来）
✅ Look at clouds! It's going to rain.
看乌云，马上要下雨。
场景 2：非出行类动作（逛街/做饭/学习）→ 只能 be going to
❌ I'm cooking dinner tonight.（cook 不是位移词，语法错误）
✅ I'm going to cook dinner tonight.
❌ I'm buying a new pen tomorrow.（buy 不是位移词）
✅ I'm going to buy a new pen tomorrow.
📝 做题口诀
眼见征兆马上发生 → 只用 be going to
出门行程定好日期 → 位移动词用 be doing
临时随口做个决定 → 直接选用 will do
极简做题口诀：
① 动词不是 go/come/leave/fly 这类出行词 → 只用 be going to
② 是出行动词，但只是心里想想、没订票 → be going to
③ 是出行动词，车票/约定全部定死、不改期 → be doing
④ 看见眼前征兆，马上要出事 → 只能 be going to
🔀 if 引导四大条件句 完整超详细讲解 核心
前置基础概念
if 条件句永远分为两部分：
• if 从句：提出假设的条件（放前/放后都可以）
• 主句：满足条件后产生的结果
四大类核心区分标准：假设是否真实、发生的时间、实现可能性
一、零条件句 Zero Conditional（100% 必然发生，客观真理）
1. 标准时态公式
If + 一般现在时，主句 + 一般现在时
2. 使用场景
描述永恒不变的客观规律、科学常识、固定规则、机器固有功能。无时间限制，过去/现在/未来只要满足条件，结果一定会发生。翻译常用「只要……就……」
3. 例句拆解
If you heat water to 100℃, it boils.
只要把水加热到100摄氏度，水就会沸腾。（科学定理，永远成立）
If you touch fire, you get burned.
只要触碰火焰，你就会被烫伤。
If you don't water plants, they die.
不给植物浇水，它们就会枯死。
4. 关键特征 & 易错点
• 主句绝对不能出现 will/can/may/might/be going to 这类表将来的词
• 只讲永久规则，不针对某一次、某一天的单独情况
❌ 错误：If you heat water, it will boil.
✅ 标准零条件句：If you heat water, it boils.
二、第一条件句 First Conditional（将来真实假设，高概率发生）
1. 标准时态公式
If + 一般现在时，主句 + will/can/may/might/be going to + 动词原形
2. 使用场景
针对未来某一次特定场景做出假设，条件有很大概率实现，用于计划、警告、承诺、可能性推测。
3. 主句换词含义（不同情态动词语气差异）
will：确定会做
can：能够、可以（具备条件就能做）
may/might：也许、可能（不确定，概率偏低）
be going to：提前计划好将要做
👉 主句换用 can/may/might/be going to 依然属于第一条件句，只是语气不同，不属于零条件句
4. 分层例句
✅ will（确定）：If it is sunny this Sunday, I will visit the flea market.
如果这周日天晴，我就去逛跳蚤市场。（本周日单次计划）
✅ can（能够）：If I finish homework early, I can watch TV.
如果我早点写完作业，我就能看电视。
✅ might（也许）：If it rains tomorrow, we might stay at home.
如果明天下雨，我们或许会待在家里。
✅ be going to（计划）：If I have money, I am going to buy a new bag.
如果我有钱，我打算买个新包。
5. 硬性语法规则
if 从句表将来时，永远不能用 will，只能用一般现在时：
❌ If I will have time, I go shopping.
✅ If I have time, I will go shopping.
6. 和零条件句核心区别
零条件句：永久通用  |  第一条件句：只针对未来单次事件
零：If it rains, the ground gets wet.（只要下雨地面就湿，永久规律）
第一：If it rains this Saturday, I can stay home.（仅限本周六这一次）
三、第二条件句 Second Conditional（现在/将来虚拟，几乎不可能）
1. 标准时态公式
If + 一般过去时，主句 + would/could/might + 动词原形
⚠️ 特殊规则：所有人称 be 动词统一用 were（正式语法）
If I were you / If he were rich
2. 两大使用场景（全部是空想，和现实相反）
场景 1：与【当下现在】的真实事实相反
现实是目前不具备这个条件，只是幻想当下改变现状。
真实：I don't have much money now. 我现在没钱。
虚拟：If I had much money, I would travel abroad.
如果我现在有钱，我就出国旅行。（暗含现实：我没钱，做不到）
真实：I am not tall. 我个子不高。
虚拟：If I were taller, I could play basketball well.
我要是高点，篮球就能打得很好。
场景 2：【未来极低概率】的幻想
中彩票、超难实现的愿望
If I won the lottery tomorrow, I would quit my job.
要是我明天中了彩票，我就辞职。（中奖概率极低，纯幻想）
3. 重要易错提醒
if 从句里的过去式不代表过去发生，只是虚拟语气的语法标记，专门表示「现在和现实相反」
If I had money ≠ 我过去有钱，意思是：我现在要是有钱（现在没钱）
四、第三条件句 Third Conditional（过去虚拟，无法挽回的遗憾）
1. 标准时态公式
If + had + 过去分词（had done），主句 + would/could/might + have + 过去分词（would have done）
2. 使用场景
针对已经结束、无法更改的过去进行假设。现实中过去已经发生了某件事，现在幻想当初换一种做法，会有不一样的结果，自带后悔、惋惜情绪。
3. 例句对照（真实过去 vs 虚拟假设）
真实：I got up late yesterday, so I missed the bus.
我昨天起晚了，错过了公交车（事情已经发生，无法重来）

虚拟：If I had got up early yesterday, I wouldn't have missed the bus.
我昨天要是早起，就不会错过公交车了。
真实：She didn't study hard, so she failed the exam last week.
虚拟：If she had studied hard, she could have passed the exam.
她当初要是努力学习，上周本来能及格。
4. 时间区分核心
第二条件句 → 聚焦现在、未来，现状能看见，只是空想改变当下
第三条件句 → 聚焦昨天、上周、从前，事情已成定局，无法补救
五、第二 vs 第三条件句直观对比（同一件事，不同时间）
第二条件句（现在没空）
If I had free time now, I would help you.
我现在要是有空，我就能帮你。
第三条件句（昨天没空）
If I had had free time yesterday, I would have helped you.
我昨天要是有空，当时就能帮你了。
六、四大条件句汇总表格
类型从句时态主句时态可能性适用场景
零条件句 一般现在时 一般现在时 100% 一定发生 客观真理、永久规则
第一条件句 一般现在时 will/can/may/be going to do 大概率发生 未来单次真实计划、警告
第二条件句 一般过去时 did would/could/might do 几乎不可能 当下现实相反、未来空想
第三条件句 had done 过去完成时 would/could/might have done 完全不可能（过去已定） 对过去的后悔、假设
📝 万能做题区分口诀
① 永久道理，主句无将来词 → 零条件句
② 未来单次计划，主句带 will/can/may → 第一条件句
③ 现在现状相反，从句过去式，主句 would + 原形 → 第二条件句
④ 过去已成定局，从句 had done，主句 would have done → 第三条件句
核心区分维度：
• 时间：现在/未来 vs 过去已成定局
• 真实性：100%真实 vs 大概率 vs 几乎不可能 vs 完全不可能
• 从句时态：现在时 → 零/第一  |  过去时（did）→ 第二  |  过去完成时（had done）→ 第三
📊 频率副词排序 MC36
never 0% → rarely → seldom → occasionally → sometimes → often → usually → always 100%
位置规则：实义动词前，be动词后
✅ We seldom fasten seat belts.（实义动词前）
✅ I am usually busy.（be动词后）
⚡ sometimes 位置灵活，可放句首/句中/句尾
🔄 双宾语 to / for 高频
公式：动词 + 人 + 物 = 动词 + 物 + to/for + 人
介词含义常见动词例句
to 方向/传递：东西从A到B lend, loan, give, pass, send, show, tell Pass me the salt.
= Pass the salt to me.
for 目的/服务：东西为B准备 buy, make, book, bring Buy me a coffee.
= Buy a coffee for me.
记忆口诀：传递给某人→to；为某人做→for
🎭 -ed / -ing 形容词系列 易错
动词-ed（人感受）-ing（事物属性）搭配介词
disappoint disappointed 失望的 disappointing 令人失望的 at sth / with sb / about sth
excite excited 兴奋的 exciting 令人兴奋的 about sth
surprise surprised 惊讶的 surprising 令人惊讶的 at sth / about sth
interest interested 感兴趣的 interesting 有趣的 in sth
tire tired 疲惫的 tiring 累人的 of sth 厌烦 / from sth 劳累
bore bored 无聊的 boring 乏味的 with sth/sb
核心规律：-ed 描述人的感受 → "我感到……"
-ing 描述事物本身 → "这个东西令人……"
介词口诀：at反应、with对人、about事情、in兴趣、of厌烦、from原因
⚡ 情态动词 must / have to 家族 MC38
表达含义例句
must 必须（主观） I must finish this today.
mustn't 严禁、不准 You mustn't park here.
have to / has to 不得不（客观） I have to work overtime.
had to 过去不得不（+过去时间） I had to stay late yesterday.
don't have to 不必（≠mustn't） You don't have to come early.
❌ 不能说 haven't to → 用 don't have to
❌ must 没有过去式 → 过去用 had to
💬 情态动词：请求 & 建议 MC18
分类一：提出请求（礼貌等级）
礼貌级别情态动词例句
最礼貌委婉Could / Would / MayCould you please pass the salt?
Would you mind opening the window?
May I borrow your pen?
日常口语随意Can / WillCan you help me with this?
Will you grab me a coffee?
⚠️ Would you mind doing sth.
mind 后必须接动名词 doing，不能接 to do！
Would you mind to open ❌ → Would you mind opening ✅
分类二：给出建议
语气强度情态动词例句
直接、较强建议should / ought toYou should see a doctor.
We ought to leave soon.
柔和、委婉建议might / could / canYou might want to think about it again.
Perhaps we could try the other route.
You can ask your teacher for help.
🤝 borrow / lend / loan MC38
词方向搭配例句
borrow 借入（别人→我） borrow sth from sb Can I borrow a pen from you?
lend 借出（我→别人） lend sb sth = lend sth to sb
过去式 lent		 I can lend you my stapler.
loan 正式借出/贷款 loan sb sth = loan sth to sb The bank loaned me the money.
❌ 不能说 borrow sb sth → 只能 borrow sth from sb
📍 介词速查 基础
介词核心含义典型用法
in大时间/大地点/沉浸里面in 2024 / in Beijing / in the morning / in cash
on具体某天/平面/施加影响on Monday / on the table / on sale / tax on...
at钟点/小地点/瞄准目标at 8:00 / at the corner / good at
for原因/目的/持续时间for 3 years / for you / famous for
of所属/组成/包含a cup of tea / made of wood / experience of
to朝向/对应/通往go to school / listen to / give...to
with伴随/使用/对抗with a hat / cut with a knife / angry with
by方式/交通/截止时间by bus / by credit card / by Friday
记忆口诀：大时间地点in，具体某天on，钟点小地点at，原因目的for，所属组成of，朝向对应to，伴随使用with，方式交通by
🌳 从句体系概览 进阶
从句类型功能常用连接词例句
主语从句 作主语 that / whether / what What she said is true.
宾语从句 作宾语 that / if / whether / 疑问词 I know that he is honest.
定语从句 修饰名词（≈形容词） who/whom/which/that/whose/where/when The man who is talking is my teacher.
状语从句 修饰动词/全句（≈副词） when/while/because/if/although/so...that He is so kind that everyone likes him.
定语从句 vs 同位语从句：
定语从句：that 在从句中充当成分 → The news that he told me
同位语从句：that 不作成分，解释内容 → The news that he is coming
⏱️ when vs while 易混
whenwhile
搭配瞬间动作 / 进行时进行时（持续动作）
含义"这时突然……""与此同时……"
例句I was running when I tripped.While I was running, I tripped.
🚪 open/close vs turn on/turn off 中式英语重灾区
判断规则：有没有通电/水流？
open / close
物理开合，无电无水
open the door🔊开门
open the window🔊开窗
open the book🔊打开书
open the fridge🔊开冰箱门
close the door🔊关门
close the box🔊关上盒子
turn on / turn off
通电/水流，启动开关
turn on the light🔊开灯
turn on the TV🔊开电视
turn on the AC🔊开空调
turn on the tap🔊开水龙头
turn off the phone🔊关手机
turn off the computer🔊关电脑
❌ open the light / open the AC / open the tap
❌ close the TV / close the phone / close the computer
✅ 以上全部改用 turn on / turn off
一句话判断：这个"开/关"有没有通电或控制水流？→ 有就用 turn on/off，没有就用 open/close。
特别注意：水龙头看似"拧开"，本质是开关控制水流 → turn on the tap，不是 open！
📝 语法散点集
very / so / too 用法区别
词用法例句
very只修饰形容词/副词，不修饰动词very helpful ✅ / very like ❌
soso + adj. + that... "如此……以至于"He is so kind that everyone likes him.
tootoo + adj. "太……（过度）"
too...to... "太……以至于不能"		The suit is too expensive.
at all 用法
句型含义例句
not … at all一点也不I don't care about it at all.
疑问句 + at all到底、究竟Do you keep in touch at all?
Not at all.不客气（口语）—Thank you. —Not at all.
to do vs doing
形式含义例句
to do没做、将要做、目的I want to go. / use phone to chat
doing做过、正在做、习惯爱好I enjoy reading. / recommend doing
suggest 用法（易错！）
用法正误例句
suggest + doing✅ 正确I suggest going to the park.
suggest + 名词✅ 正确I suggest a plan. / He suggested Paris as our destination.
suggest + to do❌ 错误（中式英语）I suggest to go ❌ → I suggest going ✅
⚠️ suggest 后不能接 to do！这是高频中式英语错误。
中文"建议去做"容易直译成 suggest to do，但英语里 suggest 直接接 doing 或名词。
拓展：suggest that sb. (should) do sth.（虚拟语气，should可省）
I suggest that he (should) study harder.
make + 宾语 + 形容词
结构含义例句
make + sth. + adj.使某物变得…make sth. easier 使某物更简单
make + doing + adj.让做某事变得…make using a smartphone much easier
do/does/did 强调语气（口语）
时态结构例句
一般现在时
主语三单		does + 动词原形Your mom does care for you!
一般现在时
其余主语		do + 动词原形I do like your new jacket!
一般过去时did + 动词原形I did finish my homework yesterday!
⚠️ 硬性规则：do/does/did 后的实义动词必须用原形！
I did finished ❌ → I did finish ✅
一般过去时被动语态
结构例句
单数：was + 过去分词The watermelon was eaten by me.
复数：were + 过去分词The apples were bought yesterday.
主动 → 被动：I ate the watermelon. → The watermelon was eaten by me.
keep + doing 持续/反复做
含义特点例句
动作不停重复带厌烦/持续情绪He kept answering me every time I spoke.
持续进行一直做某动作Anna kept pushing the gas pedal.
used to do 过去习惯（现已不做）
结构含义例句
used to + 动词原形过去常做，现已不做I used to drink alcohol, but now I quit.
be used to + doing习惯于（仍在做）I am used to waking up early.
⚠️ used to do ≠ be used to doing
过去习惯（已停） vs 现在习惯（仍在）
every time 引导时间状语从句
词性含义例句
连词短语每当、每次Every time I ask you a question, the man replies to me.
引导从句后接完整句子Every time I speak, he kept answering me.
易混词辨析
易混词区别例句
breath / breathen.呼吸 / v.呼吸take a deep breath / breathe slowly
message / massagen.消息 / n.按摩send a message / get a massage
rent / rentalv.租用 / adj.租赁的rent a car / rental agreement
licence / license英式执照 / 美式执照driver's licence (UK)
量词搭配（群体名词）
量词适用对象例句
a flock of一群鸟a flock of birds flying south
a herd of一群牛羊牲畜a herd of cows grazing
a school of fish一群鱼a school of fish swimming
专有名词（首字母必须大写）
专有名词含义
President of the United States美国总统
White House白宫
Forbidden City紫禁城
Tiananmen Square天安门广场（中国）
🔤 s后清辅音浊化发音 MC35
规则示例发音变化
s + p → /b/spoon /spuːn/ → 听起来像 /sbuːn/p浊化成b的发音
s + t → /d/student /ˈstjuːdənt/ → 听起来像 /ˈsdjuːdənt/t浊化成d的发音
s + k → /g/sky /skaɪ/ → 听起来像 /sgaɪ/k浊化成g的发音
s + tʃ → /dʒ/matchbox /ˈmætʃbɒks/ → 读作 /ˈmædʒbɒks/⚠️ 不是/ˈmætʃbɒks/！这是本单元重点
⚠️ matchbox读/ˈmædʒbɒks/而非/ˈmætʃbɒks/！s后面的清辅音要浊化，这是自然发音规则。
🔗 并列连词 and/or 规则 MC4
语境用词例句
肯定句并列andI like jazz and pop. 两种都喜欢
否定句/疑问句并列orI do not like rock or blues. 两种都不喜欢
选择疑问orDo you like jazz or rock? 选一个
否定两个选项orHe has no brothers or sisters. 没有兄也没有妹
⚠️ 否定句并列必须用 or，不能用 and！
I do not like rock and blues ❌ → I do not like rock or blues ✅
🎯 目的状语 in order to vs so that MC35
结构接什么例句区别
in order to+ 动词原形He slapped his face in order to stay awake.接动词原形，不构成从句
so that+ 完整句子(含can/could)He propped his eyelids open so that he could stay awake.接完整从句，含情态动词
同义改写：He opened the windows in order to get fresh air. = He opened the windows so that he could get fresh air.
📈 比较级修饰词 much/a lot MC4
修饰词含义例句注意
much……得多My family is much bigger than yours.much + 比较级，强调差距大
a lot……得多 (= much)It is a lot quieter here.a lot = much，口语中更常用
a little / a bit……一点It is a little cheaper.a little + 比较级，差距小
even甚至更……It is even colder today.even + 比较级，出乎意料
⚠️ much/a lot 修饰比较级，不能修饰原级！
much big ❌ → much bigger ✅ / a lot quiet ❌ → a lot quieter ✅
⏰ 4类时态全覆盖 MC35
时态结构例句(MC35语境)用法
一般过去时did（过去式）He drove at night.过去完成的动作
过去进行时was/were + doingHe was driving when he fell asleep.过去某一刻正在做
一般现在时do/doesDrivers get tired at night.普遍事实/规律
现在完成时have/has + doneHe has pulled over at a rest area.过去动作影响现在
MC35叙事时间线：一般过去时(主线) → 过去进行时(正在做) → 一般现在时(总结) → 现在完成时(影响)
📍 almost 固定位置 MC35
规则例句说明
almost 放在主语后、动词前He almost fell asleep.almost + 动词，修饰动作
almost 放在否定词前He almost did not make it.almost + not，差一点没做成
❌ 不能放在句末fell asleep almost ❌almost是副词，不能放在动词后
❌ not…any more MC35
结构例句含义
not … any moreHe is not sleepy any more.再也不瞌睡了（状态改变）
not … anymoreI do not live there anymore.再也不住在那里了（美式拼写）
区别：not any more = 不再（英式，可分开写）/ not anymore = 不再（美式，一个词）
含义相同，都表示"以前是这样，现在不再如此"
🏆 最高级表排行 MC4
结构例句含义
the + 最高级 + in/ofI am the eldest in my family.我是家里最年长的（排行第一）
the + 最高级 + of the + 数She is the youngest of the three siblings.她是三兄妹中最小的
the second + 最高级He is the second eldest.他排行第二
排行表达：the eldest(老大) → the second eldest(老二) → the youngest(最小)
❗ What引导感叹句 MC4
结构例句含义
What + a + adj. + 单数名词！What a lively family!多么热闹的家庭啊！
What + adj. + 不可数名词！What great news!多么好的消息啊！
What + adj. + 复数名词！What beautiful pictures!多么美的照片啊！
⚠️ What a + 单数可数名词（必须加a）！
What lively family ❌ → What a lively family ✅
✋ 动词固定搭配 S+V+O+to MC35
结构例句含义
apply sth to sthHe applied balm to his temples.把清凉油涂在太阳穴上
prop sth open with sthHe propped his eyelids open with matchsticks.用火柴杆撑开眼皮
block sth with sthThe matchsticks blocked his eyes.火柴杆挡住了视线
S+V+O+to 模式：主语 + 动词 + 宾语 + to + 方向/目标位置
apply ... to ... 是"把……涂在/施加到……上"的固定搭配
🧭 问路方向副词不加介词 MC39
错误正确规则
go to therego therethere/here/home 是副词，前面不加介词to
go to homego homehome作副词时前面不加to
arrive at homearrive homearrive + 副词地点直接连接
go to upstairsgo upstairsupstairs/downstairs 也是副词
记忆口诀：there/here/home 前面不加to，它们自带"到"的意思！
📊 do vs be 判断规则 MC39
情况用do/does/did用be(am/is/are/was/were)
实义动词作谓语Does she like jazz?❌ 不用be
形容词作表语❌ 不用doIs she tired?
名词作表语❌ 不用doAre they siblings?
有助动词已用do/does/did已用be(进行/被动)
判断公式：谓语是实义动词 → 用do/does/did
谓语是be+形容词/名词 → 用be本身
📝 名词性从句详解 从句体系
类型作用引导词例句
主语从句整个从句作主语that / whether / whatWhat she said is true. 她说的是真的
宾语从句整个从句作宾语that / whether / if / whatI know that he is honest. 我知道他诚实
表语从句整个从句作表语that / whether / becauseThe truth is that he lied. 事实是他撒了谎
同位语从句解释名词内容that（不可省略）The fact that he won surprised everyone. 他赢了这件事震惊所有人
名词性从句本质：整个从句相当于一个名词，充当主/宾/表/同位语四种角色
🔍 定语从句详解 从句体系
类别引导词用法例句
关系代词who修饰人（作主语/宾语）The man who is talking is my teacher.
whom修饰人（只作宾语）The person whom I met was kind.
which修饰物The car which he drove was old.
that修饰人或物（通用）The book that I read was great.
whose表示所属关系The student whose name is Tom won.
关系副词when修饰时间I remember the day when we met.
where修饰地点This is the place where he parked.
why修饰原因Tell me the reason why he fell asleep.
限制性 vs 非限制性定语从句
类型特点例句
限制性（无逗号）不可缺少，删除后意思不完整The man who is talking is my teacher.
非限制性（有逗号）补充说明，删除后意思完整My father, who is 60, likes jazz.
⚠️ 非限制性定语从句不能用 that，只能用 who/which！
My father, that is 60 ❌ → My father, who is 60 ✅
⏱️ 状语从句详解 从句体系
类型引导词例句含义
时间状语when / while / before / after / until / sinceWhile he was driving, he fell asleep.当……正在……
地点状语where / whereverWhere there is a road, there is a rest area.哪里有路，哪里就有休息区
原因状语because / since / asBecause he was tired, he pulled over.因为……
目的状语so that / in order thatHe propped his eyelids open so that he could stay awake.以便……
结果状语so … that / such … thatHe was so tired that he fell asleep.太……以至于……
条件状语if / unless / as long asIf you feel sleepy, pull over.如果……
让步状语although / though / even thoughAlthough he tried hard, he fell asleep anyway.虽然……但是……
方式状语as / as if / as thoughHe drove as if he was fine.好像……
📊 从句对比分析 从句体系
对比项区别例句A例句B
that vs whatthat仅连接，不充当成分
what充当主/宾，有实际含义		I know that he is honest.（that无含义）What he said is true.（what=the thing that）
which vs that
(定语从句)		which只修饰物
that修饰人或物
非限制性只用which		The book which I read …（限制性可用）The book, which I read, …（非限制性只用which）
定语从句 vs
同位语从句		定语从句修饰名词
同位语从句解释名词内容		The fact that he told me …（he told me修饰fact）The fact that he won …（he won解释fact内容）
判断方法：删掉that后从句——
如果从句完整（缺修饰）→ 定语从句
如果从句不完整（缺主宾）→ 同位语从句
📍 核心介词用法速查 介词体系
介词核心含义主要用法例句
in大范围/沉浸里面①大时间（年月季节）
②大地点（城市国家）
③沉浸状态
④用…方式		in 2024 / in Beijing / in the morning / in cash / in a hurry
on具体某天/平面接触①具体某天/某日
②平面/接触面
③关于/影响
④在售/操作		on Monday / on the table / on sale / tax on … / on the phone
at钟点/小点/瞄准①钟点时间
②小地点（角/门/站）
③瞄准/擅长		at 8:00 / at the corner / good at / aim at
for原因/目的/持续①持续时间
②目的/为了
③原因/因为
④代表		for 3 years / for you / famous for / stand for
of所属/组成/关于①所属关系
②组成/包含
③关于/描述		a cup of tea / made of wood / experience of …
to朝向/对应/到达①方向/朝向
②对应/给
③到达（大地点）
④伴随不定式		go to school / listen to / give … to / want to do
with伴随/使用/对抗①和…一起
②用…工具
③对抗/面对
④具有/带着		with a hat / cut with a knife / angry with / a house with a garden
by方式/经过/截止①方式/手段
②交通方式
③截止时间
④旁边		by bus / by credit card / by Friday / stand by
记忆口诀：
in大圈里泡着→大时间/大地点/沉浸
on面上贴着→具体天/平面/接触
at针尖扎着→钟点/小点/瞄准
for为了多久→目的/持续/原因
of属于什么→所属/组成/关于
to箭头指向→朝向/到达/给
with人手拿着→伴随/工具/对抗
by旁边经过→方式/交通/截止
📊 频率副词 MC36
频率排序(低→高): never(0%) → rarely(5%) → seldom(10%) → occasionally(15%) → sometimes(25%) → often(50%) → usually(70%) → always(90%)
规则例句注意
实义动词前I seldom fasten my seat belt.🔊频率副词放在实义动词前面
be动词后I am usually busy.🔊频率副词放在be动词后面
sometimes灵活Sometimes I walk. / I sometimes walk. / I walk sometimes.🔊句首/句中/句尾均可
💡 at all 用法 MC36
场景例句含义
否定句I do not use this app at all.🔊一点也不;根本不
疑问句Do you keep in touch at all?🔊到底;究竟
口语回应Not at all.🔊不客气;没关系
⏰ 过去进行时+when MC13&40
经典句型: 主语 + was/were doing + when + 一般过去时
含义: 正在做……这时突然……
连接词后接时态例句
when瞬间动作(一般过去时)I was running when I tripped.🔊
while持续动作(过去进行时)While I was running, I tripped.🔊
动词双写规则: 重读闭音节+辅元辅结尾 → 双写末尾辅音+ed
trip → tripped / step → stepped / stop → stopped
🔄 反身代词 MC13&40
人称反身代词例句
ImyselfI hurt myself.🔊
youyourselfDid you hurt yourself?🔊
he/shehimself/herselfShe hurt herself.🔊
weourselvesWe hurt ourselves.🔊
theythemselvesThey hurt themselves.🔊
记忆口诀: 反身代词 = 对应人称代词 + self/selves
常见搭配: hurt oneself / by oneself / enjoy oneself
⚡ used to vs be used to MC14&12
结构含义例句易错
used to do过去常常做(现在不再)I used to do cardio every day.🔊to后接动词原形
be used to doing习惯于做I am used to eating early.🔊to后接动名词doing
📐 so...that & the+比较级 MC14&12
结构含义例句
so + adj/adv + that + 句子太…以至于…It was so expensive that I could not afford it.🔊
the + 比较级, the + 比较级越…越…The closer, the better.🔊
🎯 主谓一致-不定代词 MC31&11&20&26
铁律: everyone / nobody / somebody / everything / nothing 全部视作第三人称单数，谓语动词用三单形式
Everyone needs a phone. ✅ / Everyone need a phone. ❌
Nobody knows the answer. ✅ / Nobody know the answer. ❌
🔑 one of + 复数名词 MC31&11&20&26
结构: one of + 复数名词 + 单数谓语动词
One of my friends is tall. ✅ / One of my friends are tall. ❌
拓展: strength n.优点;力量 / weakness n.缺点
I think one of my strengths is creativity.
⚠️ unless = if not MC31&11&20&26
unless 除非 = if not 如果不
引导条件状语从句，主句用将来时，从句用一般现在时
I will not go unless it is sunny. = I will not go if it is not sunny.
🌟 wish sb + 名词 MC31&11&20&26
结构: wish sb. + 名词 (双宾语结构)
I wish him luck. ✅ / I wish him lucky. ❌
wish后接人+名词表祝愿，不能接形容词
👀 look系列辨析 MC31&11&20&26
短语含义辨析
look for🔊寻找强调动作过程，未找到
find🔊找到强调结果，已经找到
look at🔊观看;仔细看at强调方向
⏳ It takes + 时间 + to do MC31&11&20&26
结构: It takes + 时间 + to do sth
It 是形式主语，真正主语是后面的 to do 不定式
It takes 2 hours to drive there. 开车去那里要2小时。
🔄 keep on doing = continue MC31&11&20&26
keep on doing sth = continue doing sth 坚持持续做某事
介词 on 后接动名词 doing
He kept on running even though he was tired.
📍 there be 就近原则 MC31&11&20&26
铁律: there be 句型，be动词单复数看后面第一个名词
There is a pen and two books on the desk. ✅ (看pen，单数)
There are two books and a pen on the desk. ✅ (看books，复数)
📝 名词+to do后置定语 MC31&11&20&26
结构: 名词 + to do (不定式作后置定语)
翻译: 可供…的 / 需要…的
things to look at = 可以观赏的事物
a problem to solve = 需要解决的问题
🚫 not vs no — have的否定 语法核心
核心规则: not 是副词 → 只能否定动词；no 是形容词 → 直接修饰名词
结构用法例句说明
no + 名词no直接修饰名词I have no friends.🔊最简洁，no=not any
haven't got + any + 名词英式否定haveI haven't got any friends.🔊英式英语常用have got
don't have + any + 名词美式否定haveI don't have any friends.🔊美式英语常用do/does have
❌ 绝对不能: hasn't friends / haven't time / haven't money
因为 not 是副词，不能直接放在名词前面否定名词！
✅ 正确: has no friends / has no time / has no money
💡 记忆口诀: not配动词（is not / do not），no配名词（no time / no money）
have的否定三选一: have no X / haven't got any X / don't have any X
🐺 动物量词与状语从句 MC15
语法点规则例句
动物量词搭配flock(羊/鸟)、herd(牛/鹿/象)、pack(狗/狼)、school(鱼)、swarm(蜂/蝶)、colony(蚁/蜂)a flock of sheep / a herd of cattle / a pack of wolves / a school of fish
宾语从句动词后 that 引导宾语从句，that 可省略He learned (that) no one trusts liars.
时间状语从句when/after/once 引导，主从句统一用一般过去时After they heard his shout, they ran up the hill.
让步状语 even wheneven when = 即使，引导让步状语从句No one believes a liar even when he tells the truth.
not...at all 完全否定放在否定句末尾，加强"完全不"语气They didn't find any wolf at all.
see sb doing sth感官动词 + 宾 + doing = 看见某人正在做We can see villagers running towards the boy.
不定式作形式主语It is + 形容词 + to do sthIt would be fun to trick the villagers.
过去进行时was/were + doing，表达过去某刻正做某事The villagers thought the boy was tricking them.
🏥 看医生常用语法 健康
语法点规则例句
should 建议should + 原形 = 应该做；shouldn't = 不应该You should see a doctor. / You shouldn't eat spicy food.
need to 必须need to + 原形 = 需要做（比should更强）You need to take this medicine three times a day.
How long + 现完How long have/has + sb. + done = 多久了How long have you had this pain?
have a + 症状描述病痛必须加 a（不可数除外）I have a headache / a fever / a cold.
hurt vs ache vs painhurt=动词疼；ache=持续性隐痛；pain=名词痛My head hurts. / I have a stomachache. / I feel pain in my back.
If I were you, I'd虚拟语气第二条件句，表"如果我是你"If I were you, I'd get some rest.
🪞 Would like to 礼貌表达 语法
结构用法例句
I'd like to + do礼貌表达"我想做…"（比 I want to 更礼貌）I'd like to check in, please.
I'd like + 名词礼貌表达"我想要…"（餐厅/酒店常用）I'd like a double room for two nights.
Would you like to?礼貌邀请"您要不要…"Would you like to try the local food?
Would you like + 名词?礼貌提供"您要…吗"Would you like a window seat?
I'd like = I would like 缩写，是旅行中最常用的礼貌句型！
餐厅点餐：I'd like a burger. ✅ / I want a burger. ❌（太直白）
酒店入住：I'd like to check in. ✅ / I want to check in. ❌（不礼貌）
🛎️ Could / May I 礼貌询问 语法
结构礼貌程度旅行场景例句
Could I + do?最礼貌（推荐旅行用）Could I have the menu, please?
May I + do?正式礼貌（出入境/酒店）May I see your passport?
Can I + do?日常口语（朋友间）Can I pay by card?
Could you tell me?礼貌请人帮忙（问路）Could you tell me how to get to the station?
旅行中尽量用 Could/May替代 Can！
Could I = 我能不能…（请求） / Could you = 您能不能…（请人帮忙）
两者都比 Can 礼貌10倍，在外国服务场合尤其重要！
🌍 Have been to 旅行经历表达 语法
结构含义例句
have been to + 地点去过（已回来，有经历）I've been to Paris three times.
have gone to + 地点去了（还在那，没回来）She's gone to the airport.（她还在机场）
have been in + 地点 + for在某地待了多久I've been in London for 5 days.
never been to从未去过（否定经历）I've never been to Japan. How about you?
been to vs gone to是旅行必备区别：
been to = 去过回来了 → 谈经历 ✅
gone to = 去了还没回 → 说别人去了哪 ✅
聊天破冰：Have you ever been to...? 你去过…吗？
📋 so far vs by now 完整区分 新
一、so far
核心意思：到目前为止；迄今为止（从过去一直延续到说话此刻）
字面：到现在这个节点为止，全程累计的情况
1. 固定搭配时态（必考）
绝大多数搭配现在完成时 have/has done
2. 两层场景
场景用法例句
累计数量/进度 So far + 现在完成时，强调总共、累计 So far, I have learned 3000 English words.
到目前为止，我已经学了 3000 个英语单词。
目前情况评价 So far + 一般现在时，描述当下状态 So far, everything is good.
到目前为止，一切顺利。
3. 位置灵活
句首或句尾都可以：
So far, no one has come. = No one has come so far.
二、by now
核心意思：到现在这个时候；按理此刻应该……
自带两层隐含语气：
① 说话人心里有预期，觉得这件事现在本该发生
② 现实往往和预期相反（暗含失望、疑惑）
1. 时态搭配
语气结构场景
肯定/预期should have done虚拟，本该做却没做（暗含失望）
客观陈述现在完成时 have done说话当下的客观结果
口语一般现在时随意的日常表达
2. 例句（突出"预期反差"）
They should have arrived by now.
按说到这个点他们早就该到了。（现实：人还没来，失望）

By now, you know I hate lying.
到现在你本该清楚我讨厌说谎。

I've read 10 pages by now.
到这会儿我已经看完 10 页了。
三、核心 4 大区别（做题直接区分）
维度so farby now
语义侧重点 累计、全程到现在
纯客观统计，无期待对比		 到此刻（带心理预期）
觉得现在理应完成，常暗含没达到预期
固定场景 统计数字、进度、累计次数
So far, we have sold 100 books.		 推测、本该完成、吐槽没按时
He should be home by now.
时态差异 几乎固定 现在完成时 常搭配 should have done（虚拟本该）
经典对比 So far, I've written 2 articles.
只说总数，无期待		 By now, I should have finished 5.
实际只写2篇，达不到预期
四、极简记忆口诀
算总数、看进度，客观累计用 so far；
有期待、嫌太晚，本该完成用 by now。
五、同类型时间表达 全面对比
表达语体风格时态隐含预期例句
so far 口语高频 现在完成时 🚫 无，纯累计 I have learned 3000 words so far.
up to now 书面通用 现在完成时 🚫 无，纯累计 Up to now, we haven't received any reply.
until / till now 通用 现在完成时 🚫 无，纯累计 I have never tried sushi until now.
as yet 正式，多用于否定 现在完成时（否定） 🚫 无 As yet, no decision has been made.
to date 学术、作文 现在完成时 🚫 无 To date, 500 people have signed up.
by now / by this time 口语高频 should have done / 现完 ✅ 有，暗含"本该做完" He should be here by now.
by + 具体时刻 过去 / 将来截止点 将来完成时 / 过去完成时 ✅ 有时间预期 I will have finished by 5 PM.
up to + 过去年份/日期 截止过去时间 过去完成时 had done 🚫 客观截止 Up to 2019, I had never left China.
💡 快速分类技巧
不带预期（纯统计）：so far / up to now / until now / as yet / to date → 都配现在完成时
带预期（暗含对比）：by now / by + 时刻 → 配 should have done 或 will have done
看截止时间定：截止现在→ 现在完成时 | 截止过去→ 过去完成时 | 截止将来→ 将来完成时
🔧 短语动词 Phrasal Verbs 完整分类 MC32
分类规则例句
动词+副词
（可拆分）		宾语为普通名词：可放中间或末尾pick up clothes = pick clothes up
宾语为人称代词：只能放中间！✅ pick you up / ❌ pick up you
常见短语：pick up/call off/tear upcalled off the meeting = called the meeting off
动词+介词
（不可拆分）		短语整体不能拆开✅ look for them / ❌ look them for
常见短语：look for/look after/look intolook after the dog / look into that spy
⚠️ 核心区分：人称代词(you/them/him/her)放动副之间 pick you up；动介短语代词放最后 look for them
📐 被动语态 & 反义疑问句 MC19&20
语法点结构公式例句
被动语态be + 动词过去分词The meeting was called off. 会议被取消了。
高频不规则take→taken, hear→heard, read→read, break→brokenMy phone was broken. 我的手机弄坏了。
反义疑问句前肯后否，前否后肯You don't know, do you?
主句主语→人称代词You want it, don't you?
I don't care, do I?
💡 反义疑问句口诀：前肯后否，前否后肯；主语变代词，时态要一致
🤔 三选一：do / be动词 / 都不用 高频痛点
一、先判断句子「有没有动作动词」
句子类型用谁例句
状态/身份/特征
（后接名词·形容词·介词短语，无动作）		 be 动词
(am/is/are/was/were)		 She is a doctor.
We are from China.🔊
有动作动词
（like/eat/go...），且没有其他助动词		 do / does
(三单用 does)		 He does like jazz.
I don't eat meat.🔊
已有 will/can/must/have(完成)/be(进行) 都不用
它们自带提问/否定		 I can swim. → I can't swim.
She has finished.🔊
二、疑问句怎么造
原句提问规则
You are tall.🔊Are you tall?🔊be 提前
She likes tea.🔊Does she like tea?🔊加 does，动词还原
They can go.🔊Can they go?🔊情态动词提前，不加 do
三、否定句怎么造
原句否定规则
He is a teacher.🔊He isn't a teacher.🔊be + not
I like it.🔊I don't like it.🔊don't/doesn't + 原形
She has eaten.🔊She hasn't eaten.🔊has + not，不加 do
💡 决策三步：① 状态/身份 → be；② 有动作动词且无其他助动词 → do/does；③ 已有 will/can/must/have(完成)/be(进行) → 都不用，它们自己搞定。
⚠️ 经典错误：Do you are...?（be 和 do 不能同框）｜ I don't can...（情态动词前不加 do）｜ Does she likes...?（does 后动词必须还原）
🔤 名词复数 & f/fe 结尾变形规则 MC8&1
规则：以 f / fe 结尾的名词，变 f/fe → v，再加 -es
例：life → lives、knife → knives、leaf → leaves、wolf → wolves
He lives in the suburbs.（live 的三单也拼 lives，注意与名词复数同形）
⏪ 一般过去时 MC08
时间标志：last week、last vacation、yesterday
be 动词：am/is → was；are → were
实义动词变过去式：go → went、stay → stayed、love → loved、buy → bought
I was on vacation. / She went to San Francisco.
⏰ 一般现在时 MC01
结构：主语 + 动词原形 / 动词三单
疑问句：Do / Does + 主语 + 动词原形
铁律：句中有实义动词（work / commute / take / live），不能配 am/is/are
只有描述身份、状态、特征时才用 be 动词
How do you commute to work?
⏱️ It takes sb. + 时长 + to do MC01
结构：It takes + 人 + 时间段 + to do sth.（做某事花费某人多久）
It 是形式主语，真正主语是后面的 to do 不定式
It takes me 40 minutes to get to work. 我上班路上要40分钟。
The commute takes 40 minutes.
🚀 be about to do（即将） MC12
含义：正要、马上就要发生的动作
结构：be (am/is/are) about to + 动词原形
He is about to leave. 他马上就要离开了。
just as he's about to unzip his pants 就在他正要拉开拉链时
🔗 that 引导宾语从句 MC12
结构：动词 + that + 完整陈述句，口语中 that 可省略
常见动词：pretend / think / know / say
He pretends (that) he doesn't know me. 他假装不认识我。
he pretends that his swimming trunks are a handkerchief
🚫 一般过去时否定句 MC08
固定结构：主语 + didn't + 动词原形
注意：didn't 后动词必须还原原形！
I didn't go anywhere. 我哪儿都没去。
I didn't have enough money. 我没有足够的钱。
🍰 易混：dessert vs desert MC8&1
dessert /dɪˈzɜːt/ 甜点（两个 s）
desert /ˈdezət/ 沙漠（一个 s）
记忆：甜点让人想"再来两份(ss)" → dessert；沙漠荒凉只有一个 s
🌿 现在分词作伴随状语 MC12
作用：现在分词短语补充说明主语的状态，表主动、伴随
...he sees another man sitting very close to him
sitting 修饰 another man，表示"正紧挨着他坐着"的伴随状态
puts them back into his pocket 是并列谓语，补充说明后续动作
📖 used to 过去习惯 MC05
结构说明例子
used to + 动词原形🔊过去反复发生、现在不再I used to dig in the garden.🔊
didn't use to🔊否定（用 use，不是 used）I didn't use to like coffee.🔊
Did you use to...?🔊疑问句Did you use to live here?🔊
💡 used to 只有过去式，没有现在时！现在习惯用 I usually...
📖 because / so / and 连词 MC21-22
词作用用法
because🔊表原因...because there are many bugs.🔊
so🔊表结果There are many bugs, so I bring repellent.🔊
and🔊并列句连接They returned and spent their honeymoon.🔊
💡 中文"因为…所以…"→英语只能用其一！Because..., so... 是典型中式错误。
📖 How 疑问句 MC10
句型问什么例句
How big...?🔊面积 / 大小How big is your house?🔊
How tall...?🔊高度How tall is his dad?🔊
How old...?🔊年龄How old is she?🔊
How far...?🔊距离How far is the store?🔊
💡 How 后接形容词决定问法，不能混用。
🔄 过去进行时 + 一般过去时 语法
两个动作同时发生 / 一个长动作被短动作打断时，长动作用过去进行时（was/were + doing），短动作 / 打断用一般过去时（did）。
while + 过去进行时（持续）
While I was sleeping, the phone rang.
While she was cooking, I set the table.
when + 一般过去时（打断）
I was sleeping when the phone rang.
He called while I was showering.
📌 规则：while 接「持续时间」→ 用过去进行时；when 接「某个时间点 / 打断」→ 常用一般过去时。
💡 两个同时进行的长动作可都用过去进行时：While she was cooking, I was setting the table.
❌ 常见错误：While I watched TV, he came. → ✅ While I was watching TV, he came.
🏠 房产 How 疑问句 MC10
问法例句
How big...?🔊How big is your house?🔊
How tall...?🔊How tall is his dad?🔊
How old...?🔊How old is she?🔊
How far...?🔊How far is the store?🔊
🏡 描述家乡 · 形容词反义词 & 拓展短语 MC10
反义词对拓展短语
busy ↔ unbusy🔊the hustle and bustle 喧嚣热闹🔊
modern ↔ traditional🔊the cost of living 生活成本🔊
young ↔ old🔊born and raised 土生土长🔊
fast-paced ↔ slow-paced🔊square meter 平方米🔊
crowded ↔ quiet🔊do a facial 做面部护理🔊
wet/humid ↔ dry🔊natural sights 自然风光🔊
inclusive ↔ exclusive🔊1/2/3-tier city 一/二/三线城市🔊
clean ↔ polluted🔊—🔊
safe ↔ dangerous🔊—🔊
convenient ↔ inconvenient🔊—🔊
interesting ↔ boring🔊—🔊
stressful ↔ relaxing🔊—🔊
📖 MC01 工作职业 · 语法 Two Jobs, Two Lives
sound + 形容词 描述印象；sound like + 名词/代词/从句 表示相似或比喻
📌 That movie sounds interesting. / It sounds like it's going to rain.
sound 后接形容词，sound like 后接名词或从句；易混淆两者用法
📖 MC02 购物 · 语法 I'll Take It!
fit 指尺寸/形状合适；suit 指款式/颜色好看、衬人
📌 This shirt is too tight; it doesn't fit me. / Blue is your color! That dress really suits you.
fit 强调合不合身，suit 强调好不好看，两者常混淆
📖 MC03 餐厅点餐 · 语法 May I Take Your Order?
用 will / would 提出请求；would 比 will 更礼貌
📌 What would you like? I'd like the veggie burger. / I'll have a mango salad.
点餐时用 I'd like / I'll have 表达自己；问对方用 Would you like...?，would 更委婉
📖 MC04 家庭家人 · 语法 I Didn't Know That
量词（Quantifiers）表示多少：all(100%)、most(80-90%)、a lot of/many(50-70%)、some/a few(10-30%)、no/not any(0%)
📌 Most families in Australia live in the suburbs. / I have a few friends.
可数/不可数名词搭配不同；no 等于 not any
📖 MC05 飞机遇险 · 语法 The Smartest Man
过去进行时(was/were+ing)表过去某时正在进行的动作；一般过去时表已完成的动作；短动作打断长动作时两者连用
📌 A doctor, a businessman, a father, and a son were flying on a small plane. / The plane began to fall.
when 引导从句中，长动作(过去进行)被短动作(一般过去)打断，如 I was walking when I saw a cat.
📖 MC06 选择餐厅 · 语法 Where Should We Eat Tonight?
最高级表示'最……'，形容词前加 the；单音节加 -est，多音节用 most，不规则 good→best, bad→worst
📌 He is the tallest person in the country. / She's my best friend.
有所有格时不加 the，如 my best friend；双音节以 -y 结尾变 y 为 i 加 -est
📖 MC07 外貌描述 · 语法 He's Really Good Looking
用 in+衣服 表示穿着；with+名词 表示特征或配饰（眼镜、背包、发型等）
📌 a man in a black coat / a girl with long hair
描述发型顺序：长度+质感+颜色+hair，如 long straight black hair
用 What does he/she look like? 询问外貌；How tall / How old 分别问身高年龄
📌 What does she look like? She's tall, with black hair. / How old is she? She's about 32.
问年龄可用 in one's thirties 或 about + 数字；有所有格时最高级前不加 the
📖 MC08 旅行假期 · 语法 I was on Vacation
在讲述过去的事时，涉及现在仍属实的一般事实或电影/书情节，可用一般现在时
📌 I loved it! It's a really pretty city. / Titanic was released in 1997. It tells the story of Jack and Rose.
描述电影/书情节常用现在时；仍真实的事实也用现在时，如 My sister lives there.
📖 MC09 旅行游玩 · 语法 My Feet Are Killing Me!
现在完成时用于谈论过去不确定的经历（不说明何时发生）；一般过去时用于谈论过去特定时间已完成的动作（通常说明时间）
📌 I've been here for about a week. / I lost my key yesterday.
现在完成时结构 have/has + 过去分词；一般过去时规则动词加 -ed，不规则动词用过去式。两者常混用：先问经历（完成时），再追问细节（过去时）。
How long have you been...? 现在完成时询问在某地/状态持续的时间
📌 Have you been in Orlando long?
与 how long 连用强调动作从过去持续到现在，答语常用 for + 时间段。
📖 MC10 家乡描述 · 语法 Where Do You Call Home
程度副词（adverbs of degree）表示事物强度，通常放在所修饰的形容词、副词或动词之前
📌 It's actually a fairly large town. / He's walking too slowly. / He has just finished.
常见程度副词由弱到强大致为：not very, quite, a bit, fairly, rather, pretty, very, really, somewhat, extremely。注意 fairly 与 rather 的区别与位置。
📖 MC11 倒霉趣事 · 语法 A Bad Day
限定性关系从句用 who/that 指人，提供关于人的必要信息
📌 A firefighter is a person who puts out fire. / He's the man that I met at the conference.
关系代词后接主语时可省略 who/that（如 The assistant we met）；后接动词时不可省略（如 The assistant that helped us）。
原因状语从句用 because 合并两个句子，说明原因
📌 I want to go to Hawaii because it is warm and beautiful.
because 引导的从句表示直接原因，语气比 since/as 强；可放在主句之后。
📖 MC12 海滩趣事 · 语法 At the Beach
现在分词作简化关系从句，相当于主动关系从句 who is doing
📌 The man driving the car is my friend. (= The man who is driving the car is my friend.)
现在分词（动词+ing）作后置定语表主动或进行；可把 who is/are + V-ing 简化为 V-ing。
方位介词 in / at / on 表示位置
📌 Little Red sits on the top. / They are playing in a big house. / at the corner of the house.
in 用于大范围或封闭空间（in a car, in China）；on 用于表面或线上（on the top, on a wall）；at 用于具体点（at the door, at the bus stop）。
📖 MC13 幽默娱乐 · 语法 That's Hilarious
用 I bet... 表达对他人感受的理解或十分肯定的推测，意为'我敢肯定/我猜'
📌 I lost my wallet yesterday. — I bet that was stressful!
可回应故事（表共鸣），也可在很有把握时发起陈述（I bet he's exhausted）。
一般现在时疑问句与简答，并用宾语代词（me/him/her/them）
📌 Do you like country music? Yes, I do. / They like them a lot.
疑问句用 do/does；简答 Yes/No + 主语 + do/does；否定用 don't/doesn't；宾语代词替代名词避免重复。
📖 MC14 租房 · 语法 Rent an Apartment
How + 形容词 用于描述性提问（年龄、高度、距离、尺寸等）
📌 How big is your house? / How far is the shop? / How old are you?
结构：How + Adj. + is/are + 主语？常结合 many/long/much 等构成疑问，如 How many bedrooms? How long does it take?
📖 MC15 童话寓言 · 语法 The Boy Who Cried Wolf
宾语从句用 that 引导：主语 + 动词 + that...，或 主语 + be + 形容词 + that...
📌 The shepherd boy finally learned that no one believes a liar. / I'm afraid that I can't help you.
that 在口语中常省略；glad/sorry/afraid 等形容词后接 that 从句表达情绪。
📖 MC16 药房买药 · 语法 The Pharmacist Knows Best
情态动词表请求与建议：用 can/could/will/would/may 提请求；用 should/ought to/might/can/could 提建议
📌 Could you please pass the menu? / You should see a doctor.
请求中 Could/Would/May 更礼貌正式，Can/Will 较随意；建议中 should/ought to 较直接，might/could 更委婉。
📖 MC17 健身运动 · 语法 You're in Great Shape
too ... to ... 结构：表示某特性（形容词/副词）过度，从而阻止动作发生
📌 I'm too busy to go to the gym today.
句型为 主语 + be/动词 + too + 形容词/副词 + to + 动词原形；不可与 so...that 混用，如需强调结果用 so...that。
📖 MC18 健康计划 · 语法 Making Health Plans
suggest 的用法：后可接动名词(-ing)、that 从句、名词或疑问词；比 advise 更口语化
📌 I suggest eating more fruit. / I suggest (that) you see a doctor.
suggest 后接动词必须用 -ing（不能接 to do）；that 从句多用虚拟语气，可省略 should，如 I suggest you see a doctor。
📖 MC19 洗手间趣事 · 语法 The Restroom Story
被动语态 (Passive Voice)：be + 过去分词，强调动作的承受者
📌 He was killed in a car accident. / The building has been destroyed.
当主语是动作的承受者时用被动；时态由 be 动词体现（was/were/has been/will be 等）。主动变被动时宾语变主语，动词变 be+done。
📖 MC20 能力才艺 · 语法 What Can You Do?
反义疑问句 (Tag Questions)：陈述句后加简短疑问，用于确认已知信息；前肯后否，前否后肯
📌 You don't like it, do you? / He does know that, doesn't he?
主句有助动词时用同一助动词；无助于动词（一般现在/过去）时用 do/does/did；注意人称与时态一致。
📖 MC21 露营装备 · 语法 Decide What You Need for Camping
so 与 because 的连用规则：because 表原因，so 表结果，同一句不可同时用 because 和 so
📌 Mary was sick last week so she saw a doctor. / I was late because I overslept.
中文常“因为…所以…”连用，但英文中 because 和 so 只能用其一，不可同时出现在一个句子里。
📖 MC22 工作时间 · 语法 What Hours Do You Work?
时间介词 at / on / in 的区别：at+具体时刻或特殊时段；on+星期/节日/日期；in+一天中的时段/年/月/季节
📌 Let's meet at 9:00. / She visits her parents on Friday. / I work in the morning.
at 用于 4:00 pm、noon、midnight、night；on 用于 Monday、my birthday、September 16th；in 用于 morning、April、spring、2025。
📖 MC23 生日礼物 · 语法 The Birthday Present
双宾语动词 send / buy：send sth to sb = send sb sth；buy sth for sb = buy sb sth
📌 My mom sent a gift to me. = My mom sent me a gift. / I bought a parrot for her. = I bought her a parrot.
to 侧重方向，for 侧重目的；间接宾语指人，直接宾语指物。
imagine 的三种用法：imagine doing sth / imagine sb doing sth / imagine that + 句子
📌 I imagine living on a farm. / I imagine him singing. / I imagine that she will like it.
imagine 后不接 to do。
cost vs spend：cost 主语是物（物 + cost + 人 + 钱）；spend 主语是人（人 + spend + 钱 + on sth）
📌 The phone cost me 5000 yuan. / I spent 5000 yuan on the phone.
cost 过去式仍是 cost，不能写成 costed。
虚拟语气：与现在事实相反的假设，if 从句用过去式（be 用 were），主句用 would + 动词原形
📌 If I were the woman, I would buy insurance for my mom.
口语中偶尔说 If I was，但正式写作用 were。
enough 的位置：enough + 名词；形容词/副词 + enough；enough of + 限定词 + 名词
📌 enough money / special enough / slowly enough / enough of your noise
名词前 enough 前置，形容词/副词后 enough 后置。
📖 MC24 考试通过 · 语法 I Passed!
do / does / did 表强调：用助动词加强主要动词语气，后接动词原形，口语中重读
📌 I do like your new jacket! / Your mom does care for you! / I did finish my homework yesterday!
do（现在）/does（三单）/did（过去）后必须接动词原形；用于肯定句加强语气，不可用于否定或疑问。
📖 MC25 算命占卜 · 语法 Seeing a Fortune Teller
用 will 一般将来时表达对未来的预测
📌 We will get married in September.
will + 动词原形表示对将来事情的预言；否定用 won't，疑问把 will 提前。
用 wh- 疑问词 + will 提问未来细节
📌 When will she go to university?
可结合 when / where / what / who with 等疑问词询问时间、地点、事件、人物。
📖 MC26 问路·速配 · 语法 We need some directions / Made for Each Other
there is / there are 表示存在，搭配 one/any/some 及方位介词
📌 Is there a laundromat near here? Yes, there's one across from the shopping center.
there is 接单数/不可数，there are 接复数；方位介词 in / on / next to / across from / between 等。
表示同意的句型：so/neither + 助动词 + I 及其等同表达
📌 I can't play the piano. — Neither do I. / Me neither.
肯定用 so do I / I do too / me too；否定用 neither do I / I don't either / me neither。
📖 MC27 临终愿望 · 语法 Last Wish
so...that... 结构表示因果（程度导致结果）
📌 He was so sick that he knew he didn't have much time.
句型为 So + 形容词/副词 + that + 从句；前面是原因（程度），that 引出强烈的结果。
📖 MC28 请假·健康饮食 · 语法 I Can't Come In Today / Making healthy choices
祈使句（imperative clauses）用于建议、请求、命令
📌 Have fun. / Don't be late.
通常无主语，用动词原形；否定加 Don't，常用于给他人建议或指令。
have to 与 must 表示必要性；mustn't 表示禁止；过去用 had to
📌 You must eat more vegetables. / You mustn't eat junk food.
have to 偏客观必须，must 偏主观必须；禁止用 mustn't；过去式用 had to（不能用 must）。
📖 MC29 相亲速配 · 语法 Speed Dating
形容词比较级（comparatives）表示两者之间的差异
📌 Dogs are more intelligent than rabbits.
结构为 主语 + 动词 + 比较级 + than + 宾语；单音节加 -er，以 y 结尾改 i 加 -er，多音节用 more，不规则 good→better、bad→worse、far→farther/further。
📖 MC30 目的地选择 · 语法 Where Should I Go?
疑问词 + to 不定式 作宾语（wh-clause + to-infinitive）
📌 I'm still thinking about where to go on my vacation.
结构为 动词 + 疑问词(what/who/which/when/where/how) + to do；常用于 decide, know, discuss 等动词后。
📖 MC31 园艺挖土 · 语法 Dig Up the Garden
关系从句中 where 指代地点
📌 That's the place where the bodies are buried.
where 引导定语从句修饰表示地点的名词（如 place, garden, stadium），说明在该地点发生的事。
📖 MC32 面试求职 · 语法 The Interview
短语动词（phrasal verbs）的可分/不可分及代词位置
📌 You can tear these want ads up. / I'll pick you up at 8:00.
有些可分离（call off, tear up），代词必须放中间；有些不可分离（look after, look into），宾语位置固定。
📖 MC33 求职面试 · 语法 Who's the Best for the Job?
动名词与不定式表技能/能力/意愿：be good at / be skillful in / have experience in + 动名词(-ing)；be willing to / be able to + 不定式(to do)
📌 I am good at writing reports. He is willing to work overtime.
谈论技能、能力和意愿时，be good at/skillful in/have experience in 后接动名词，be willing/able to 后接动词不定式。
📖 MC34 单身生活 · 语法 The Single Man
第二条件句(Second Conditional)：If + 一般过去时, ... would + 动词原形，用于假设、想象或不太可能发生的情况及其结果
📌 If you found a girl who was just like your mom, she would definitely like her.
if 从句用一般过去时（be 常用 were），主句用 would + 动词原形；表示与现在/将来事实相反的假设。
📖 MC35 开车提神 · 语法 Mr. Bean's Car Journey
目的表达 in order to 与 so that：in order to + 动词原形表目的（否定 in order not to）；so that + 从句，常配合 can/would 等情态动词
📌 Mr. Bean used the matchsticks to prop his eyelids open so that he could stay awake.
in order to 后接动词原形，so that 后接从句；两者都表“为了/以便”，so that 强调结果从句。
📖 MC36 手机APP · 语法 Important Apps
频率副词(Adverbs of Frequency)：通常放在主语和动词之间，或情态/助动词与主要动词之间；频率由低到高：never/seldom/rarely/occasionally/sometimes/often/usually/always
📌 She always goes to work by bus. He is sometimes late for work.
频率副词位置错误如 'She go to work always' 或 'He sometimes is late' 是错的；应置于主语后或助动词后。
📖 MC37 销售推销 · 语法 The Good Salesman
第一条件句(First Conditional)：If + 一般现在时, will + 动词原形，用于谈论可能实现的将来条件及其结果
📌 If this machine doesn't pick up all the dirt, I will eat all of it!
if 从句用一般现在时表将来可能条件，主句用 will + 动词原形表结果；可用于威胁、承诺或预测。
📖 MC38 借用文具 · 语法 May I Borrow Your Stapler?
将来时表达：will（说话时临时决定、承诺、预测）；be doing（已安排好的固定计划）；be going to（说话前已决定的计划或基于证据的预测）
📌 I'll make her a gift. We are celebrating at 7 PM tonight.
will 强调当场决定/承诺；be doing 强调既定的安排（如已订票）；be going to 强调事前计划或有证据的预测。
📖 MC39 跳蚤市场 · 语法 Flea Market
双宾语动词(Double Object Verbs)：结构为 动词+间接宾语+直接宾语，或 动词+直接宾语+to/for+间接宾语；带 to 的动词有 give/lend/offer/pass/send/show/tell/write 等，带 for 的有 book/bring/buy/make/get/keep 等
📌 My wife sent me an email. / My wife sent an email to me.
间接宾语指人、直接宾语指物；两种结构可互换，注意 to/for 的选用依动词而定。
📖 MC40 抢劫意外 · 语法 I was Minding My Own Business
时间状语从句 when 与 while：一次性、不持续的动作用 when（when + 一般过去时, 过去进行时）；进行中的动作/一段时间用 while（while + 过去进行时, 一般过去时）
📌 When Tony Steel came in, I was having dinner. / She hurt herself while she was trying to stop the crime.
when 强调某一时刻发生的短暂动作打断持续动作；while 强调两个动作同时进行，从句须用进行时态。
形容词最高级规则（MC06）

不规则变化：good → better → the best；bad → worse → the worst

规则① 单音节词 +er/est：tall → taller → tallest；cheap → cheaper → cheapest

规则② 辅音+y结尾 变y为i+er/est：busy → busier → busiest；noisy → noisier → noisiest

规则③ 多音节(≥3) 前加more/most：interesting → more interesting → the most interesting

句式：主语 + be + the + 最高级 + 范围(in/of...)

例：It is the quietest restaurant in the city.

fit vs suit 区分（MC02）

fit：侧重尺寸大小是否合身。例：The medium size doesn't fit me.

suit：侧重风格/肤色/气质是否适配。例：This dress suits you well.

介词搭配：look great on you（人身上用 on）

现在完成时：haven't seen ... for + 时间段（好久没见...）

例：We haven't seen each other for ages. 我们好久没见了。

I wish 虚拟语气（MC27）

规则：表达现实无法实现的愿望，从句时态倒退一格

现在愿望：I wish + 一般过去时（与现实相反）

例：I wish I had fair skin. 我真希望我皮肤白皙（现实不是）。

过去遗憾：I wish + 过去完成时 (had done)

例：I wish I hadn't gotten pale skin. 我真不该面色这么苍白。

I wish that we were different from each other.

I wish I could inherit his wealth.

注意：fair skin（褒义·好看的白皮）vs pale skin（贬义·生病苍白）不可混用

📝 MC29 & MC30 核心语法 必考
结构音标含义例句
enjoy / like / recommend / suggest + doing🔊enˈʤɔɪ laɪk rekəˈmend səˈʤest duɪŋ喜欢/推荐/建议做某事I recommend visiting temples.
watch / see / hear sb + doing🔊wɔʧ si hir sb* duɪŋ看见/听见某人正在做I watched performers dancing.
advise sb + to do🔊ədˈvaɪz sb* tɪ du建议某人做某事She advised me to try sashimi.
as + 形容词/副词 + as🔊ez 形容词/副词* ez和……一样as good as the local food
比较级 + than🔊比较级* ðən比……更……Lily is calmer than Sarah.
have got to = must🔊hæv gɑt tɪ məst必须，得You've got to try sashimi.
listen to🔊ˈlɪsən tɪ倾听（to 不可省）listen to the guide
疑问词 + 不定式🔊疑问词* 不定式*where to go / what to dothink about where to go
relaxing (事物) / relaxed (人)🔊rɪˈlæksɪŋ 事物* rɪˈlækst 人*令人放松的 / 感到放松的a relaxing trip / I feel relaxed.
-ing 形容词修饰事物（a relaxing trip），-ed 形容词修饰人（I feel relaxed）。
🏷️ 主题词汇
🏠 租房 & 生活 MC14
英文音标时态/复数中文

😰 情绪表达 MC14
英文音标中文搭配用法
nervous🔊/ˈnɜːvəs/紧张的be nervous about 对……感到紧张
anxious🔊/ˈæŋkʃəs/焦虑的be anxious about 对……感到焦虑
upset🔊/ʌpˈset/沮丧的be upset about/with 对……感到沮丧
stressed🔊/strest/有压力的be stressed out 压力很大 / be stressed about 对……感到压力
furious🔊/ˈfjʊəriəs/狂怒的be furious with sb 对某人愤怒 / be furious at sth 对某事愤怒
disappointed🔊/dɪsəˈpɔɪntɪd/失望的be disappointed with/at/about 对……感到失望
confident🔊/ˈkɒnfɪdənt/自信的be confident about/in 对……有信心
inspired🔊/ɪnˈspaɪəd/受鼓舞的be inspired by 被……所鼓舞
💡 情绪形容词用法公式：be + 形容词 + 介词 + 对象
例句：I'm nervous about the interview. 我对面试感到紧张。
例句：She's furious with her boss. 她对老板很愤怒。
例句：He's stressed out about work. 他工作压力很大。

📊 频率副词完整排序 MC36
频率排序(低→高)
0% never /ˈnevə(r)/ 从不 5% rarely /ˈreəli/ 很少 10% seldom /ˈseldəm/ 不常 15% occasionally /əˈkeɪʒnəli/ 偶尔 25% sometimes /ˈsʌmtaɪmz/ 有时 50% often /ˈɒfn/ 经常 70% usually /ˈjuːʒuəli/ 通常 90% always /ˈɔːlweɪz/ 总是
位置规则
✅ 实义动词前: I seldom fasten my seat belt.
✅ be动词后: I am usually busy.
✅ sometimes位置灵活，可放句首/句中/句尾

📢 祈使句详解 语法
类型结构例句
肯定祈使句动词原形开头（无主语）Sit down, please. / Open the door.
否定祈使句Don't + 动词原形Don't be late. / Don't worry.
Let's 祈使句Let's + 动词原形 = 一起做某事Let's go! / Let's take a break.
Be + 形容词Be + adj. = 保持…状态Be careful! / Be quiet!
Please 礼貌Please + 祈使句 / 祈使句 + pleasePlease sit down. / Come in, please.
No + doing（禁止）No + 动名词 = 禁止做某事No smoking. / No parking.
祈使句核心：省略主语 you，直接用动词原形开头。否定加 Don't，礼貌加 Please。
Let's = Let us 缩写，表"让我们一起…"，反意疑问用 shall we？
✈️ 坐飞机 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
boarding pass/ˈbɔrdɪŋ pæs/登机牌Here is my boarding pass.
check in/ʧek ɪn/办理登机/入住I need to check in for my flight.
departure/dɪˈpɑrʧər/出发/离港The departure time is 10 AM.
arrival/ərˈaɪvəl/到达/到港The arrival gate is B7.
gate/geɪt/登机口Boarding at Gate 12.
carry-on随身行李Only one carry-on bag allowed.
luggage / baggage/ˈləgɪʤ/ /ˈbægɪʤ/行李Where can I drop my luggage?
delay/dɪˈleɪ/延误The flight is delayed by 2 hours.
cancel/ˈkænsəl/取消The airline cancelled my flight.
security check/sɪˈkjʊrəti ʧek/安检Please go through security check.
take off/teɪk ɔf/起飞The plane will take off in 10 minutes.
land/lænd/降落We will land at 3 PM.
seat belt/sit belt/安全带Please fasten your seat belt.
turbulence/ˈtərbjələns/颠簸/气流We're experiencing some turbulence.
aisle / window seat/aɪəl/ /ˈwɪndəʊ sit/过道/靠窗座位I'd prefer a window seat.
机场常用缩写：DCA = Departures（出发）/ ARR = Arrivals（到达）
记住顺序：check in → security check → boarding → take off → land → baggage claim

WiFi password/aɪ aɪ ˈpæswərd/WiFi密码What's the WiFi password?
breakfast included/ˈbrekfəst ɪnˈkludɪd/含早餐Is breakfast included in the price?
酒店入住流程：I'd like to check in. → 给预订号 → 付押金 → 拿房卡 → 询问WiFi
退房：I'd like to check out. → 归还房卡 → 结账
🍽️ 点餐用餐 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
menu/ˈmenju/菜单Could I see the menu, please?
order/ˈɔrdər/点餐/下单I'd like to order the steak.
appetizer / starter/ˈæpətaɪzər/ /ˈstɑrtər/开胃菜/前菜We'll start with an appetizer.
main course/meɪn kɔrs/主菜The main course is grilled salmon.
dessert/dɪˈzərt/甜点Would you like dessert?
bill / check/bɪl/ /ʧek/账单（英/美）Could I have the bill, please?
tip/tɪp/小费It's customary to leave a tip of 15-20%.
waiter / waitress/ˈweɪtər/ /ˈweɪtrəs/男/女服务员Excuse me, waiter?
serve/sərv/上菜/服务They serve breakfast until 10 AM.
specialty/ˈspeʃəlti/招牌菜/特产What's your specialty?
take away / to go/teɪk əˈweɪ/ /tɪ gəʊ/带走/外带I'd like this to go, please.
portion/ˈpɔrʃən/份量The portion is quite large here.
点餐万能句：I'd like + 菜名（比 I want 礼貌）
美国小费：15-20%是基本，不给小费会被认为不礼貌
账单叫法：英式bill / 美式check
🗺️ 问路方向 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
turn left / right/tərn left/ /raɪt/左转/右转Turn left at the next intersection.
straight ahead/streɪt əˈhed/直走Go straight ahead for two blocks.
intersection / crossing/ɪntərˈsekʃən/ /ˈkrɔsɪŋ/十字路口It's at the intersection of Main and 5th.
block/blɑk/街区It's about 3 blocks away.
opposite / across from/ˈɑpəzɪt/ /əˈkrɔs frəm/对面The hotel is across from the park.
nearby/ˈnɪrˈbaɪ/附近Is there a restaurant nearby?
landmark/ˈlændmɑrk/地标Look for the landmark clock tower.
distance/ˈdɪstəns/距离What's the distance to the airport?
GPS / navigate/ˈnævəgeɪt/导航I'm using GPS to navigate.
on foot/ɔn fʊt/步行It's 10 minutes on foot.
问路万能句：Could you tell me how to get to...?
指路常用：Go straight → Turn left/right → It's on your left/right
距离表达：on foot 步行 / by bus 公交 / by taxi 打的
🛍️ 购物消费 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
price/praɪs/价格What's the price of this?
discount/ˈdɪskaʊnt/折扣/打折Is there a discount on this?
on sale/ɔn seɪl/打折销售This jacket is on sale — 30% off!
receipt/rɪˈsit/收据/小票Could I get a receipt?
refund/ˈrifənd/退款I'd like a refund for this.
exchange/ɪksˈʧeɪnʤ/换货/兑换Can I exchange this for a different size?
try on/traɪ ɔn/试穿May I try on this dress?
size/saɪz/尺码What size do you need?
cashier/kæˈʃɪr/收银员Please pay at the cashier.
shopping mall/ˈʃɑpɪŋ mɔl/购物中心The shopping mall is open until 9 PM.
fit/fɪt/合身/合适This fits perfectly!
bargain/ˈbɑrgɪn/便宜货/砍价That's a bargain! / Can I bargain?
购物重点：discount = 减去的百分比（10% discount = 打9折！）
试穿：try on 必须加 on（不是 try the dress ❌）
砍价：Can I get a better price? 比 Can you cheap? ✅
🛂 出入境 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
passport/ˈpæspɔrt/护照May I see your passport?
visa/ˈvizə/签证Do I need a visa to enter?
customs/ˈkəstəmz/海关Please go through customs.
declare/dɪˈkler/申报Do you have anything to declare?
immigration/ɪməˈgreɪʃən/移民/入境审查Go to the immigration counter.
border/ˈbɔrdər/边境We crossed the border at midnight.
stamp/stæmp/盖章The officer stamped my passport.
duty-free免税There's a duty-free shop at the airport.
baggage claim/ˈbægɪʤ kleɪm/行李领取Go to baggage claim at Carousel 3.
transit / layover/ˈtrænzɪt/ /ˈleɪəʊvər/过境/中转I have a layover in Dubai.
入境审查必答：What's the purpose of your visit? → Tourism / Business / Study
海关：Nothing to declare. = 没有需要申报的
记住：declare ≠ describe！是"申报"不是"描述"
💬 简单聊天 词汇
英文音标中文实用例句
How's it going?/ow's ɪt gəʊɪŋ/最近怎样？（比 How are you 更自然）How's it going? — Great, thanks!
Nice to meet you./aɪs tɪ mit ju/很高兴认识你Nice to meet you too!
Where are you from?/hir ər ju frəm/你来自哪里？I'm from China. How about you?
What do you do?/hæt du ju du/你做什么工作？I work in IT. And you?
have you been to.../hæv ju bɪn tɪ/你去过…吗？（旅行破冰）Have you been to Beijing?
I've heard that.../vi hərd ðət/我听说…（接话技巧）I've heard that the food here is amazing.
That sounds great!/hæt saʊnz greɪt/听起来不错！（积极回应）You went hiking? That sounds great!
By the way.../waɪ ðə weɪ/顺便说一下（转换话题）By the way, do you know a good restaurant?
See you around!/i ju əraʊnd/回头见！（比 goodbye 更轻松）See you around! Take care!
What's the weather like?/hæts ðə ˈweðər laɪk/天气怎么样？（万能闲聊）What's the weather like in your city?
闲聊Small Talk是西方社交核心技能！
安全话题：天气、旅行、美食、爱好（永远不踩雷）
避免话题：政治、宗教、收入（不礼貌）
接话公式：回应（That sounds great!）+ 追问（How was it?）

🏕️ 露营搭配 MC21
搭配音标含义辨析/易错
go camping🔊/gəʊ ˈkæmpɪŋ/去露营✅ 标准固定搭配，表示休闲活动
go to camp🔊/gəʊ tɪ kæmp/去夏令营❌ 不用于休闲露营；特例: go to the forest to camp
stick to🔊/stɪk tɪ/粘住;坚持stick→stuck(过去式)
pour sth into sth🔊/pɔr sth ˈɪntu sth/把某物倒入某物I poured oil into the pan.
in case of🔊/ɪn keɪs əv/万一;以防⚠️ 后接名词/名词短语，不接句子
protect sb from sth🔊/prəˈtekt sb frəm sth/保护某人免受…伤害A sun hat protects us from the sun.
There is no need to do🔊/hir ɪz nəʊ nid tɪ du/没必要做某事There is no need to take too many snacks.
I bet🔊/bet/我敢肯定I bet it did not taste good.
You bet🔊/u bet/当然;没问题回应请求的口语表达
💡 suggest用法详解 必考
结构例句易错
suggest doing sthI suggest bringing wet wipes.🔊❌ 绝对不能用 suggest to do
suggest (that) sb (should) doI suggest we (should) take a raincoat.🔊虚拟语气，should可省略
What do you recommend?你有什么推荐？🔊点餐最常用句
recommend doing sthI recommend eating more vegetables.🔊❌ 不能用 recommend to do
recommend sb to doI recommend you to try the donut.🔊正式用法，推荐某人做某事

🗺️ 问路方位 MC31&11&20&26
搭配音标含义辨析
across from / opposite🔊/əˈkrɔs frəm/ /ˈɑpəzɪt/在…正对面= right across from
go straight down + 路名🔊/gəʊ streɪt daʊn/沿着某路一直走down 沿着方向
turn right onto + 街道名🔊/tərn raɪt ˈɔntu/右转进入某街道onto 转入新道路
turn right at the + 序数词 + crossing🔊/tərn raɪt æt ðə ˈkrɔsɪŋ/在第…路口右转at 用于小地点
go straight along🔊/gəʊ streɪt əˈlɔŋ/沿着…一直走along 沿整条路行进
How can I get to ...?🔊/əʊ kən gɪt tɪ/我该如何去往…？问路万能问句
It is not very far from here.🔊/ti ɪz nɑt ˈveri fɑr frəm hir/离这里不远回答问路常用
be located in ...🔊/bi ˈləʊkeɪtəd ɪn/位于…located 固定搭配
方位介词辨析: near(大范围远距离) → close to(靠近) → next to(紧挨着,=beside) → in front of(外部前面) → behind(后面)
介词铁律: direction 全部用 in (in this direction / in all directions)
路名介词: on + 街道(静态位置) / onto + 新路(转弯进入) / at + 小地点(路口/车站)
🔗 原因&结果连接词 MC31&11&20&26
连接词含义后接
because🔊因为完整句子(有主语+谓语)
because of🔊由于名词/名词短语
due to🔊由于名词短语
thanks to🔊多亏;幸亏名词短语
so🔊所以完整句子
therefore🔊因此完整句子
as a result🔊结果完整句子
🎯 面试表达搭配 MC33&07
表达含义辨析
a good fit🔊很合适(性格/能力合拍)侧重软实力匹配
well-suited🔊非常适合书面表达，比fit正式
qualified🔊有资格的强调专业资质/硬实力
competent🔊有能力的侧重能力靠谱
capable🔊能干的侧重潜力和学习能力
suitable🔊合适的条件达标，硬性要求满足
be skillful at + 具体技能🔊擅长具体技能at + cooking/drawing
be skillful in + 抽象领域🔊擅长抽象领域in + management/language
be in charge of🔊主动负责(人管事)≠ be in the charge of(被管)
🐺 狼来了 MC15
英文搭配释义例句
look after / take care of🔊照看，照料His duty is to look after a flock of sheep.
play a trick on sb.🔊捉弄某人The boy played a trick on the villagers.
drive off🔊赶走The villagers ran to drive off the wolf.
ignore one's calls🔊无视某人的呼救They ignored his calls.
come up with an idea🔊想出主意（高级书面）He came up with an idea.
laugh one's head off🔊爆笑，笑得前仰后合The naughty boy was laughing his head off.
nothing to do but do🔊除了…无事可做There was nothing to do but watch sheep.
not...at all🔊完全不，根本（否定加强）They didn't find any wolf at all.
again and again🔊一次又一次Again and again, the boy shouted for help.
make sure (that)🔊确保He watched the sheep to make sure they were safe.
tell the truth / tell a lie🔊说实话 / 说谎No one trusts liars even when he tells the truth.
🏥 看医生 健康
英文搭配释义例句
make an appointment🔊预约I'd like to make an appointment with Dr. Smith.
see a doctor🔊看医生You should see a doctor as soon as possible.
take medicine🔊吃药（注意：不是 eat）Take this medicine after meals, three times a day.
have a fever / cold🔊发烧 / 感冒I have a fever of 38 degrees.
suffer from🔊患有…（长期）She suffers from back pain.
get better / worse🔊好转 / 恶化I hope you get better soon!
stay in bed🔊卧床休息The doctor told him to stay in bed for two days.
get some rest🔊休息一下You need to get some rest.
drink plenty of water🔊多喝水Drink plenty of water when you have a cold.
have an injection🔊打针The nurse gave him an injection in the arm.
take a temperature🔊量体温Let me take your temperature first.

🔧 短语动词速查 MC32
短语类型释义例句
pick up动副可拆接人/收拾I will pick you up at six.
call off动副可拆取消The meeting was called off.
tear up动副可拆撕碎Please tear up these ads.
look after动介不可拆照顾Who looks after the dog?
look for动介不可拆寻找Help me look for my keys.
look into动介不可拆调查The police are looking into it.
⚠️ 代词放中间(pick you up✅) vs 代词放最后(look for them✅)

🌏 MC30 旅行短语与动词搭配 MC30
英文音标中文
on my vacation🔊ɔn maɪ veɪˈkeɪʃən在我的假期
think about where to go🔊θɪŋk əˈbaʊt wer tɪ gəʊ考虑去哪里
hike up the mountains🔊haɪk əp ðə ˈmaʊntənz登山
listen to ...🔊ˈlɪsən tɪ 倾听（必须加 to）
recommend doing sth🔊rekəˈmend duɪŋ sth*推荐做某事
suggest doing sth🔊səˈʤest duɪŋ sth*建议做某事
advise sb to do sth🔊ədˈvaɪz sb* tɪ du sth*建议某人做某事
watch sb doing sth🔊wɔʧ sb* duɪŋ sth*看见某人正在做
see sb doing sth🔊si sb* duɪŋ sth*看见某人正在做
hear sb do / doing sth🔊hir sb* du duɪŋ sth*听见某人（做/正在做）
good value for money🔊gʊd ˈvælju fər ˈməni性价比高
listen to 的 to 不可省略；recommend / suggest 后接 doing，不接 to do。
💬 场景句型
❓ 提问与否定句型 do/be
想说句型解析
你是老师吗？🔊 Are you a teacher?🔊 身份句用 be 提前（无动作动词）
你喜欢爵士吗？🔊 Do you like jazz?🔊 like 是动作动词 → 用 do
她不喜欢茶？🔊 She doesn't like tea.🔊 三单否定 doesn't + 原形
你会游泳吗？🔊 Can you swim?🔊 情态动词 can 自带提问，不加 do
你从哪来？🔊 Where are you from?🔊 from 介词短语 → be 动词
💡 判断口诀：状态/身份→be；动作→do/does；已有 can/will/have→都不用。
🏠 租房问答 直接套用
句型中文解析
How much is the rent?🔊 租金多少？ 💡 how much + be + 价格类名词，询问费用的固定句型
How many bedrooms does it have?🔊 有多少间卧室？ 💡 how many + 可数名词复数 + 一般疑问句结构
Which floor is it on?🔊 在几楼？ 💡 which floor + be + 主语 + on介词，on the floor 固定搭配
How big is it in square meters?🔊 有多少平方米？ 💡 in square meters = 以平方米为单位
Is it furnished?🔊 房子带家具吗？ 💡 furnished=带家具的，be动词询问状态，租房必问
Is there an elevator?🔊 有电梯吗？ 💡 Is there + 单数名词，询问是否存在某设施
How far is the metro station?🔊 地铁站有多远？ 💡 how far + be，询问距离的固定句型
It's a 5-minute walk.🔊 步行5分钟。 💡 a 5-minute walk = 5分钟的步行路程，minute用单数形容词形式
It's 5 minutes by subway.🔊 乘地铁5分钟。 💡 by + 交通方式，表示乘坐某种交通工具
🛒 购物砍价全流程 旅游必备
阶段句型解析
问价 How much is it? / How much are they?🔊 💡 单数用is，复数用are，最基本的问价句型
What's the price of this?🔊 💡 What's the price of + 物品，另一种问价方式
砍价 Could you give me a discount?🔊 💡 Could you + 动词，委婉请求，比Can you更礼貌
Can I get a better price?🔊 💡 get a better price = 拿到更优惠的价格，口语常用
That's too expensive.🔊 💡 直接表达嫌贵，常作为砍价开场白
I can't afford it.🔊 💡 afford = 买得起，否定表达说明预算不足
成交 I'll take it.🔊 💡 I'll take it = 我买了，购物成交固定句型
We have a deal!🔊 💡 deal = 成交/协议，We have a deal = 我们达成共识
😰 情绪表达句型 日常
句型中文解析
It makes me stressed.🔊 这让我感到压力。 💡 make + 人 + 形容词，使某人产生某种情绪
It makes me nervous / anxious.🔊 这让我紧张 / 焦虑。 💡 同上结构，nervous=紧张、anxious=焦虑
It makes me upset / tired.🔊 这让我沮丧 / 疲惫。 💡 upset=沮丧、tired=疲惫，情绪形容词
I was worried that I would waste money.🔊 我担心我会浪费钱。 💡 worried + that 从句，表达担忧的具体内容
What went wrong?🔊 哪里出问题了？ 💡 go wrong = 出问题，过去式 went
Do it better next time.🔊 下次做得更好。 💡 祈使句，鼓励改进
I felt confident.🔊 我感到自信。 💡 feel + 形容词，表达当下的情绪状态
I was afraid that I couldn't pass it.🔊 我担心无法通过。 💡 afraid + that 从句，表达恐惧/担忧
🎬 兴趣爱好 口语
句型中文解析
What kind of music do you like?🔊 你喜欢哪种音乐？ 💡 What kind of + 类别，询问某类事物的偏好
I like jazz. I don't like rock or blues.🔊 我喜欢爵士。我不喜欢摇滚或蓝调。 💡 否定并列用 or 不用 and，这是一个关键语法点
How about you? / What about you?🔊 你呢？ 💡 How about / What about + you，询问对方想法的固定句型
We have a lot in common.🔊 我们有很多共同点。 💡 in common = 共同之处，have ... in common 固定搭配
Let's start with…🔊 我们从……开始。 💡 start with + 话题/事项，建议从某处开始的口语常用
🏃 犯罪新闻（过去进行时）MC40
句型中文解析
I was minding my own business.🔊 我只是在做自己的事。 💡 过去进行时：was + doing，强调当时正在发生的动作
I heard a woman yelling for help.🔊 我听见一位女士大喊救命。 💡 hear + 人 + doing（听到某人正在做某事）
Two robbers were grabbing her bag.🔊 两个劫匪正在抢她的包。 💡 过去进行时：were + doing，复数主语用 were
I was too far away to do anything.🔊 我离得太远无能为力。 💡 too ... to ... = 太……以至于不能……
While I was running, I tripped and fell.🔊 我跑的时候绊倒了。 💡 while + 过去进行时，表示"当……正在……时"
Someone stepped on my arm.🔊 有人踩到了我的胳膊。 💡 step on =踩在某物上，过去式 stepped
The robbers got kicked off the bus.🔊 劫匪被赶下公交车。 💡 get + 过去分词，被动语态的口语表达
🤝 借东西场景 MC38
类别句型解析
借入（请求） Do you have a pen I can borrow?🔊 💡 borrow + from sb，向某人借，询问是否可借
Can I borrow your stapler?🔊 💡 Can I borrow + 物品，礼貌请求借某物
借出（答应） I can lend you my stapler.🔊 💡 lend + 人 + 物品，借给某人某物
Sorry to bother you.🔊 💡 打扰别人前的礼貌用语
口语缩写 I gotta go! = I have to go!🔊 💡 gotta = got to，口语缩写，"我得走了"
⚠️ borrow vs lend 区别：borrow = 借入（向别人借）、lend = 借出（借给别人）
💪 健康生活计划句型 MC18
类别句型解析
作息习惯 I don't have a regular schedule for sleeping.🔊 💡 regular schedule = 固定作息，schedule for + 事项
I usually have brunch.🔊 💡 brunch = 早午饭（breakfast + lunch合成词）
I have a strict diet. I only eat organic & healthy food.🔊 💡 strict diet = 严格饮食，organic food = 有机食品
I don't eat refined carbohydrates like rice and noodles.🔊 💡 refined carbohydrates = 精制碳水，like + 举例
I'm very self-disciplined.🔊 💡 self-disciplined = 自律的，形容词描述人的品质
精力与社交 I don't have the energy to do any social activities.🔊 💡 have the energy to + 动词，有精力做某事
I prefer to enjoy myself.🔊 💡 prefer to + 动词，更喜欢做某事
I don't have a good work-life balance.🔊 💡 work-life balance = 工作与生活的平衡
情绪调节 When I feel sad, I eat junk food to cheer myself up.🔊 💡 cheer oneself up = 让自己开心起来，调节情绪固定短语
I used to drink a lot of alcohol, but now I quit.🔊 💡 used to + 动词 = 过去习惯（现已停止），quit = 戒掉
I smoke when I feel stressful.🔊 💡 feel stressful = 感到有压力，when + 从句表条件
睡眠 I need at least 7–8 hours of sleep to be energetic.🔊 💡 at least + 数量 = 至少，energetic = 精力充沛
After I get awake, I can never fall asleep again.🔊 💡 get awake = 醒来，fall asleep = 入睡，醒来后睡不着
I get fully charged after a nap.🔊 💡 fully charged = 满血复活，比喻用法，nap = 午睡
I get off work late, so I feel like staying up late.🔊 💡 get off work = 下班，stay up late = 熬夜
Smoking is a part of my routine.🔊 💡 a part of + 名词 = ……的一部分，routine = 日常习惯
人际关系 She treats me as friends.🔊 💡 treat sb as + 身份，把某人当作……
I'm friends with my daughter.🔊 💡 be friends with sb = 和某人做朋友，like friends
🚗 驾驶考试问答句型 MC24
类别句型解析
考试结果 She passed her driving test and got her driver's licence.🔊 💡 pass + 考试名称 = 通过考试，get + licence = 获得驾照
She took the test twice.🔊 💡 take + 考试 = 参加/参加考试，twice = 两次
驾驶习惯 Anna is good at driving farm equipment / a tractor.🔊 💡 be good at + doing，擅长做某事，farm equipment = 农用设备
She talks to herself while driving.🔊 💡 talk to oneself = 自言自语，while + doing = 当……正在……时
Anna kept pushing the gas pedal and revving the car engine.🔊 💡 keep + doing = 持续反复做，gas pedal = 油门，rev = 踩油门轰引擎
失败原因 Driving too slow and turning without looking made her fail.🔊 💡 make sb fail = 使某人失败，列举失败原因
She didn't put both hands on the wheel.🔊 💡 put hands on the wheel = 双手握方向盘，wheel = 方向盘
目的地 She wants to go to the White House.🔊 💡 want to + 地点，想去某地，White House = 白宫（专有名词首字母大写）
You can see more of the city by car.🔊 💡 by car = 开车/乘车，see more of + 地点 = 更全面了解某地
You cannot drive right up to the Forbidden City.🔊 💡 drive right up to = 开车直达，Forbidden City = 紫禁城（专有名词）
You are not allowed to drive right up to Tiananmen Square.🔊 💡 be not allowed to + 动词 = 不被允许做某事，Tiananmen Square = 天安门广场
缓解紧张 To make Anna feel less nervous, she should focus on the street, take a deep breath, chat with her driving instructor.🔊 💡 To make sb + 形容词，目的状语"为了让某人……"，列举缓解方法
🚽 洗手间误会故事 MC19
类别句型解析
完整长句 I was not the type to strike up conversations with strangers in the restroom on the side of the road.🔊 💡 strike up a conversation = 搭讪，on the side of the road = 在路边，长句拆解练习
At this point, I was starting to feel a bit weird and very uncomfortable.🔊 💡 At this point = 此时此刻，start to feel + 形容词 = 开始感到……
Every time I ask you a question, this idiot in the next stall keeps answering me!🔊 💡 Every time + 从句 = 每次……的时候，keep doing = 持续反复
口语吐槽 What the hell?🔊 💡 What the hell? = 搞什么鬼？口语吐槽惊讶/不满
To be honest = frankly speaking = honestly speaking🔊 💡 三种表达"说实话"的方式，口语常用
👋 见面寒暄基础句 必背
句型中文解析
It's great to see you!🔊 见到你真好！ 💡 It's + 形容词 + to see you，表达见面喜悦
—It's great to see you! —You too!🔊 —见到你真好！—你也是！ 💡 You too! 回应对方祝福，不是Me too（Day 2知识点）
⚠️ 回应祝福 → You too / 回应陈述事实 → Me too（比如：I like jazz. → Me too!）
✅ 现在完成时三大用法句型 MC09
用法句型解析
① 人生经历
搭配 ever / already		 I have been to Beijing.🔊 💡 have been to + 地点 = 去过某地（已回来），人生经历
I have driven a car.🔊 💡 have + 过去分词，表达做过某事的经历
Which places have you been to?🔊 💡 Which places + have you been to，询问去过哪些地方
② 持续到现在
搭配 for + 时长		 I have lived here for 5 years.🔊 💡 for + 一段时间，动作从过去持续到现在仍在进行
I have studied English for 1 year.🔊 💡 have studied + for + 时长，学习持续了一年
③ 过去影响现在 —Are you hungry? —I have eaten dinner.🔊 💡 have eaten = 吃过了，影响：现在不饿，不需要再吃
⚠️ 现在完成时不能搭配具体过去时间（in 2019❌），有明确时间用一般过去时
🚗 驾驶提神叙述句型 MC35
类别句型解析
场景开头 He was driving at night.🔊 💡 一般过去时，交代场景背景
He felt tired and sleepy during the trip.🔊 💡 feel + 形容词，描述状态；during + 名词，旅途过程中
转折叙述 However, he wanted to stay awake.🔊 💡 however 逻辑转折，引出新意图
He slapped his face, but he still dozed off.🔊 💡 but 连接转折：做了努力但还是失败
Suddenly, he burned his finger on the cigarette lighter.🔊 💡 suddenly + 一般过去时，突然事件
Just then, he had an idea — he found a matchbox and propped his eyelids open with matchsticks.🔊 💡 just then = 就在这时；have an idea = 想出主意
结局叙述 Unfortunately, the matchsticks blocked his eyes, and he fell asleep anyway.🔊 💡 unfortunately 不幸的是；anyway 无论如何（结局回归
As it turned out, the matchsticks did not help at all.🔊 💡 as it turned out = 结果原来是这样
叙事模板：背景 + 问题 → 尝试解决(However/But) → 突然事件(Suddenly/Just then) → 结局(Unfortunately/As it turned out)
🎯 目的状语句型 MC35
结构句型解析
in order to
+ 动词原形		 He slapped his face in order to stay awake.🔊 💡 in order to + do，表目的"为了做某事"
He opened the windows wide in order to get some fresh air.🔊 💡 in order to + do，目的状语放在句末
so that
+ 从句		 He propped his eyelids open with matchsticks so that he could stay awake.🔊 💡 so that + 从句(含can/could)，表目的"以便……"
He turned up the music so that he would not fall asleep.🔊 💡 so that + 从句，目的从句含情态动词
⚠️ 区别：in order to 后接动词原形，so that 后接完整句子(含情态动词)
👨‍👩‍👧‍👦 家庭对话全套口语句型 MC4
类别句型解析
照片话题 That is a great picture!🔊 💡 赞美照片的固定句型
It was taken at my graduation.🔊 💡 It was taken at + 地点/场合，描述照片拍摄场景
家庭信息 I am an only child.🔊 💡 an only child = 独生子女，介绍家庭结构
What about you?🔊 💡 What about you? 承接对话，询问对方情况
It is typical in China to have a big family.🔊 💡 typical in + 地点 = 在某地很普遍
比较描述 My family is much quieter than before.🔊 💡 much + 比较级，强调差异"安静得多"
My family is a lot bigger.🔊 💡 a lot = much，修饰比较级"大得多"
亲属方向 On my father's side, I have three cousins.🔊 💡 on one's father's/mother's side，说明父系/母系
忙碌话题 I have been busy with my work.🔊 💡 have been busy with + 事项，现在完成进行态
排行描述 I am the eldest in my family.🔊 💡 the eldest = 最年长的，最高级表排行
She is the youngest of the three siblings.🔊 💡 the youngest + of the + 数量，排行最小
感叹 What a lively family!🔊 💡 What + a + 形容词 + 名词！感叹句型
🎬 憨豆问答句型 MC35
编号问答解析
Q1 What did Mr. Bean do to stay awake while driving?🔊 💡 What did + 人 + do + 目的状语，询问某人做了什么
A1 He slapped his face, opened the windows, and turned up the music in order to stay awake.🔊 💡 并列连词and连接三个动作，in order to表目的
Q2 Why did Mr. Bean burn his finger?🔊 💡 Why did + 人 + 动词，询问原因
A2 Because he touched the hot cigarette lighter.🔊 💡 Because + 一般过去时从句，说明原因
Q3 How did Mr. Bean try to keep his eyes open after dozing off?🔊 💡 How did + 人 + 动词，询问方式
A3 He propped his eyelids open with matchsticks so that he could stay awake.🔊 💡 so that + 从句(含could)，表目的
Q4 Did the matchsticks help him stay awake?🔊 💡 Did + 人 + 动词？一般疑问句，询问结果
A4 No, they did not help at all. They blocked his eyes and he fell asleep anyway.🔊 💡 not at all = 完全没用；anyway = 无论如何
Q5 What happened in the end?🔊 💡 What happened + 时间副词，询问最终结果
A5 As it turned out, he pulled over at a rest area and took a nap.🔊 💡 as it turned out = 结果原来是这样
🍽️ 点餐场景 MC3&28&37
句型中文解析
May I take your order?🔊我可以为您点餐吗？服务员标准开场白
I would like the seafood soup, please.🔊我想要海鲜汤。I would like + 食物 + please
Do you have any whole-wheat bread?🔊你们有全麦面包吗？Do you have + any + 食物
What is your special today?🔊今日特色菜是什么？What is + your special
What do you recommend?🔊你有什么推荐？点餐最常用问句
I recommend our seafood soup.🔊我推荐我们的海鲜汤。recommend + 名词
🚗 租车对话还原 MC3&28&37
角色英文中文
AlexWelcome to Enterprise. How can I help you today?🔊欢迎来到Enterprise。有什么需要？
Mr HuI would like to hire a car.🔊我想租一辆车。
AlexHave you booked it on our website?🔊您在网上预订了吗？
Mr HuNo. I want a small car with low fuel consumption.🔊没有。我想要一辆低油耗的小车。
AlexWe have a Citroen C1 for 161.72 a week.🔊我们有一辆C1，每周161.72英镑。
Mr HuThat is a bit pricey. Do you have something cheaper?🔊有点贵。有便宜点的吗？
AlexWe have a Toyota Aygo for 110.03, unlimited mileage.🔊有丰田Aygo，110.03，不限里程。
Mr HuI will take it.🔊我选这辆。
AlexNeed insurance? 20 a day covers damage.🔊需要保险吗？每天20，含损坏保障。
AlexReturn by 5pm Feb 21st, full tank.🔊2月21日下午5点前归还，满油。
Mr HuWhere do I pick it up?🔊去哪里取车？
AlexShow your ticket at the booth. The attendant will give you the keys.🔊在柜台出示票据。工作人员会给你钥匙。
📰 犯罪新闻句型 MC13&40
句型中文语法解析
I was minding my own business.🔊我当时只是在做自己的事。过去进行时: was + doing
I heard a woman yelling for help.🔊我听见一位女士大喊救命。hear + sb + doing(听到正在做)
Two robbers were grabbing her bag.🔊两个劫匪正在抢她的包。过去进行时描述当时场景
While I was running, I tripped and fell.🔊我跑的时候绊倒摔倒了。while + 进行时 + 瞬间动作
The robbers got kicked off the bus because they did not pay.🔊劫匪因为没买票被赶下车。get + done(被动)
My co-worker is stuck in a vending machine.🔊我的同事卡在售货机里了。get stuck = 被卡住
🏆 竞赛问答句型 MC14&12
句型中文解析
Do you like taking part in competitions?🔊你喜欢参加比赛吗？like + doing 询问喜好
It can improve me and help me grow up quickly.🔊它能提升我，让我快速成长。improve + 人 + help + 人 + do
How did you feel in it?🔊你当时感觉怎么样？How did + 人 + feel
I would be sad first. Then I would learn from it.🔊我会先难过，然后从中学习。would 表虚拟/推测
I used to do cardio every day.🔊我过去每天都做有氧运动。used to do = 过去常常
The closer, the better.🔊越近越好。the + 比较级, the + 比较级
It was so expensive that I could not afford it.🔊太贵了，我买不起。so ... that ... 结果状语从句
🎵 娱乐兴趣句型 MC13&40
句型中文解析
What kind of music do you like?🔊你喜欢哪种音乐？What kind of + 名词
Let us start with classical music.🔊我们从古典音乐开始。start with + 话题
I like pop, but I do not like rock or horror.🔊我喜欢流行，但不喜欢摇滚或恐怖。否定并列用 or 不用 and
We have something in common.🔊我们有共同点。have ... in common
I am going to see a comedy this weekend.🔊这周末我要去看喜剧。be going to 表提前计划
💭 情绪表达句型 MC14&12&31
句型中文解析
It makes me stressed / nervous / anxious.🔊这让我有压力/紧张/焦虑。make + 人 + 形容词
I was worried that I would waste money.🔊我担心会浪费钱。worried that + 句子
I felt confident / sad / disappointed.🔊我感到自信/难过/失望。feel + 形容词(不用副词)
What went wrong?🔊哪里出问题了？go wrong = 出问题
I was afraid that I could not pass it.🔊我担心无法通过。afraid that + 句子
I run out of money. / I am broke.🔊我没钱了。run out of = 耗尽
🐺 图片描述 & 故事场景 MC15
场景句型例句
图片描述In the picture, I can see...In the picture, I can see a flock of sheep on the hill.
补充描述We can also see sb. doing sth.We can also see villagers running towards the hill.
职责表达One's duty is to do sth.The shepherd's duty is to look after sheep.
无所事事There is nothing to do but do sth.There was nothing to do but watch sheep eat grass.
主谓+目的sb. did sth. to make sure (that)...He watched the sheep to make sure they didn't get lost.
重复动作Again and again, 主语 + 动词...Again and again, the boy shouted for help.
故事主旨The message of this story is to...The message is to always be honest.
让步哲理No one believes... even when...No one believes a liar even when he tells the truth.
🏥 看医生问诊 健康
场景句型例句
挂号预约I'd like to make an appointment with...I'd like to make an appointment with Dr. Wang.
描述症状I have a + 症状. / My + 部位 + hurts.I have a headache. / My stomach hurts.
医生问诊What's wrong? / What's the matter?What's wrong with you today?
问持续时间How long have you had this?How long have you had this cough?
医生给建议You should / You need to / I suggest...You should drink more water and get some rest.
开药I'll prescribe you... / Take this medicine...I'll prescribe you some antibiotics. Take them twice a day.
祝康复I hope you feel better soon.Get well soon! / I hope you recover quickly.
📢 祈使句场景应用 语法
场景句型例句
课堂指令动词原形 + 宾语Open your books. / Raise your hand. / Repeat after me.
日常指令动词短语 / Be + adj.Turn off the light. / Be quiet. / Hurry up!
安全警示Don't / Watch out / Be carefulDon't touch it! / Watch out for cars! / Be careful with the knife.
邀请建议Let's / Please + 祈使Let's order some food. / Please have a seat.
标语告示No + doing = 禁止…No smoking. / No parking. / No photos.
✈️ 坐飞机场景句型 场景
场景句型具体说法
办理登机I'd like to check in for...I'd like to check in for Flight CA123 to London.
选座位I'd prefer a window/aisle seat.I'd prefer a window seat, if possible.
托运行李I'd like to check my luggage.I'd like to check two bags.
航班延误My flight is delayed.My flight is delayed by 2 hours. What should I do?
航班取消My flight was cancelled.My flight was cancelled. Can I get a refund?
安检Where is security check?Where is security check? / Do I need to take off my shoes?
登机广播Boarding at Gate...Boarding at Gate 12. Final call for Flight CA123.
机上求助Could I get...?Could I get a blanket? / Could I have some water?
🚄 交通出行场景句型 场景
场景句型具体说法
买票I'd like a ticket to...I'd like a round-trip ticket to Oxford.
问站台Which platform does...leave from?Which platform does the train to Paris leave from?
问换乘Where do I transfer?Where do I transfer to Line 2?
问地铁Which line goes to...?Which line goes to Central Station?
问公交Does this bus go to...?Does this bus go to the museum?
问票价How much is the fare?How much is the fare to downtown?
问方向Could you tell me how to get to...?Could you tell me how to get to the hotel?
问距离How far is it?How far is it from here? — About 10 minutes on foot.

入住I'd like to check in.I'd like to check in. I have a reservation under Zhang.
问WiFiWhat's the WiFi password?What's the WiFi password? / Is WiFi free?
叫醒服务Can I get a wake-up call?Can I get a wake-up call at 6 AM?
设施问题The...isn't working.The AC isn't working. / The shower is leaking.
退房I'd like to check out.I'd like to check out. Here's my room key.

结账Could I have the bill/check?Could I have the bill, please? / Separate checks, please.（分开结）

💊 药店问诊场景 MC16
场景句型解析
问症状How long have you been like this?🔊💡 现在完成时 + like this 描述状态已持续多久
描述症状I've had a bad backache since yesterday.🔊💡 have had + since + 时间点，症状从过去持续到现在
I've been coughing for about a week.🔊💡 现在完成进行时 + for + 时长，动作持续
My nose is runny and I can't stop sneezing.🔊💡 can't stop doing sth 不停做某事
药剂师建议You might want to try these capsules.🔊💡 might want to 委婉建议
You should try the cough drops, they work really well.🔊💡 should 建议 + 效果评价
💼 面试问答场景 MC32
类别句型解析
自我介绍I am the best choice for the Customer Service Staff job.🔊💡 the best choice for + 岗位
I am a good fit because I have experience dealing with customers.🔊💡 be a good fit 很适合，because + 原因状语从句
I am not suitable for the Marketing Assistant job because I do not have a university degree.🔊💡 be not suitable for 不适合，because 说明原因
提问What's the salary for this position?🔊💡 What's the salary for + 岗位
How often do you get a pay rise?🔊💡 How often 询问频率，pay rise = 加薪
What are my responsibilities for this job?🔊💡 responsibilities for + 工作
What work of yours are you most proud of?🔊💡 be proud of 引以为傲，of yours 双重所有格
🚇 MC01 通勤对话句 MC01
英文中文
I work in the city center, so it's only a short bus ride.🔊我在市中心上班，所以坐公交的路程很短。
How do you commute to work?🔊你平时怎么通勤上班？
The commute takes 40 minutes.🔊通勤路上要花费 40 分钟。
I need to take 3 subway trains.🔊我需要换乘三趟地铁。
It sounds tough.🔊听起来挺辛苦的。
You're in charge of everything.🔊所有事务都由你全权负责。
I haven't seen you in ages.🔊我们好久没见面了。
I'm working as an assistant at a clothing store in the suburbs.🔊我现在在郊区一家服装店做助理。
I'm on my feet all day.🔊我一整天都得站着工作。
🏖️ MC08 度假旅行对话句 MC08
英文中文
You were away last week, right?🔊你上周出门了，对吗？
I was on vacation.🔊我当时在外地度假。
I took a staycation this holiday instead of traveling far.🔊这次假期我选择居家短途度假，没有远行。
Where did you go?🔊你去哪里旅行了？
I went to San Francisco.🔊我去了旧金山。
How was it?🔊这次旅行体验怎么样？
My sister lives there, and I stayed with her.🔊我姐姐住在那座城市，那段时间我暂住她家。
I went sightseeing, and we went shopping every day.🔊我出门观光，我们每天都会一起逛街。
I didn't go anywhere on my last vacation.🔊上个假期我哪儿都没去。
I didn't have enough money to travel.🔊我没有足够的钱出门长途旅行。
A friend from college stayed with me for a week.🔊一位大学时期的朋友来我家住了整整一周。
We just talked and watched old movies.🔊我们只是闲聊，一起看了很多老电影。

However, just as he's about to unzip his pants, he sees another man sitting very close to him, so he pretends that his swimming trunks are a handkerchief and puts them back into his pocket.🔊然而，就在他正要拉开裤子拉链时，他看见另一个男人紧挨着自己坐着，于是他把泳裤假装成手帕，重新放回了口袋。

⛺ 露营场景句型 MC21-22
英文中文
I bring insect repellent because there are many bugs.🔊我带驱虫剂，因为虫子很多。
= There are many bugs, so I bring insect repellent.🔊= 虫子很多，所以我带驱虫剂。
💡 because（原因）与 so（结果）只能用一个，不能叠用。
🌱 土地往事句型（合并句子） MC05
原句合并后
They returned to the beach. They spent their honeymoon there.🔊They returned to the beach, where they spent their honeymoon.🔊
（同上）🔊They returned to the beach and spent their honeymoon there.🔊
💡 where 引导非限制性定语从句，指代地点 the beach。
🤝 展会商务对话句型 MC10
角色句型
销售员 SalespersonI'm ... from ... Company. I'm a sales representative.🔊
销售员This model has great features and functions.🔊
销售员It has big advantages over other products.🔊
客户 CustomerHow much is it? / How much does it cost?🔊
客户What is the wholesale price? / What is the price for bulk orders?🔊
客户How do you use it? / What are the features / functions?🔊
客户What are the pros and cons? / What are the potential benefits?🔊
客户What's the size / measurement? / What colours do you offer?🔊
客户What material is it made of?🔊
客户Is the shipping free? / What is the return policy?🔊
客户How long does it take to produce this item?🔊
🏡 描述家乡句型 MC10
框架例句
总起My hometown is a fairly large town.🔊
位置It's located in …🔊
特色It's famous for natural sights.🔊
优点Positive points: quiet, cheap, delicious food🔊
缺点Negative points: boring, crowded, expensive, stressful, dirty🔊
感受I was okay growing up here. / I've lived here for 10 years.🔊
衔接For one thing,… For another,…🔊
评价Sounds like a good place. / Sounds + 形容词 / Sounds like + 名词🔊
💡 程度副词放形容词前：absolutely / completely / extremely / really / very / quite / fairly / a bit / somewhat
