🎁 MC23 生日礼物 The Birthday Present
想说句型解析
你觉得这个礼物怎么样？🔊How do you like the present?🔊How do you like... 征求意见
我给我妈妈买了一只鹦鹉。🔊I bought a parrot for my mom.🔊buy sth for sb
这个礼物是快递寄给我的。🔊The present was sent to me by express delivery.🔊send sth to sb + by express delivery
它花了我5000元。🔊It cost me 5000 yuan.🔊cost 主语是物
我在手机上花了5000元。🔊I spent 5000 yuan on the phone.🔊spend...on...
我想象她会喜欢它。🔊I imagine that she will like it.🔊imagine that + 句子
🍽️ MC06 餐厅推荐句型 MC06
想说句型解析
这家餐厅有什么优点？🔊What's good about this restaurant?🔊What's good about... 询问优点
这家餐厅有什么缺点？🔊What's bad about this restaurant?🔊What's bad about... 询问缺点
我推荐……🔊I suggest + 餐厅名。🔊suggest + 名词/doing
它是最…的，所以很适合做…🔊It is the + 最高级，so it's great for doing sth.🔊最高级 + so 结果
很难订到位子。🔊It's hard to get a table.🔊It's hard to do sth
对素食者来说是最佳选择。🔊It's the best choice for vegetarians.🔊the best choice for sb
🛍️ MC02 服装购物句型 MC02
想说句型解析
我想买日常穿的休闲款。🔊I'm looking for something casual for daily wear.🔊look for = 寻找，daily wear = 日常穿着
这款有白色吗？🔊Does it come in white?🔊come in + 颜色 = 有某颜色款
这条棉裙你穿特别好看。🔊This cotton dress looks great on you.🔊look great on sb = 穿某人身上好看
我去收银台帮您结算。🔊I'll ring these up for you at the counter.🔊ring up = 扫码结算
这个多少钱？28.99美元。🔊How much is this? It's $28.99.🔊How much is... 问价
👨‍🍳 服务生句型 Server
场景句型解析
自我介绍🔊Hello. My name is ___. I will be your server today.🔊服务生开场白
询问点餐🔊Are you all ready to order?🔊ready to order = 准备好点餐
推荐饮品🔊How about some drinks?🔊How about + 名词 = 提议
道歉处理🔊I'm very sorry about this. I will deal with this immediately.🔊deal with = 处理
推荐菜品🔊I would recommend you to try ___. It's very delicious.🔊recommend sb to try = 推荐品尝
🍴 用餐场景句型 Dining
想说句型解析
麻烦给我一份菜单。🔊May I have a menu, please?🔊May I have... 礼貌请求
我想点一份___。🔊I'd like to order a ___.🔊I'd like to order... 点餐
店里的招牌菜是什么？🔊What is the house special?🔊house special = 招牌菜
我的菜味道太淡了。🔊There's not enough seasoning in my food.🔊not enough seasoning = 调味不足
这道菜太凉/味道淡。🔊This dish is too cold / bland.🔊too + adj. = 太…
我的菜里有异物。🔊Excuse me, there is something in my dish.🔊something in my dish = 菜里有异物
我能换成这道菜吗？🔊That sounds delicious. Can I get that instead?🔊instead = 取而代之
这份赠送免单。🔊It's on the house.🔊on the house = 免单/赠送
🚫 易错清单
🔴 致命错误（必须优先改）
错误正确说明
90% discount = 打1折90% discount = 打1折 ✅
10% discount = 打9折 ✅		discount = 减去的百分比，不是剩余
I very like it.I really like it.very 不修饰动词
My English is poor.My English is basic / limited.poor 太重，用 basic/limited
Open the light.Turn on the light.电器用 turn on/off
Play computer / phoneUse the computer / be on one's phoneplay 只用于游戏/运动/乐器
How to say?How do you say that?缺少助动词，不是完整句子
borrow sb sthborrow sth from sbborrow 后面不能直接+人+物
have a better priceget a better price砍价固定用 get
🟡 常见错误（容易踩坑）
错误正确说明
Give you.Here you go / Here you are.递东西给别人的固定说法
Me too!（回应祝福）You too!别人祝福你→You too；陈述事实→Me too
Could you have WiFi?Do you have WiFi?could you 请求动作 ≠ do you have 询问有无
I didn't hear. / What?Sorry? / I didn't catch that.没听清别说 What，太粗鲁
Thank your help.Thanks for your help.thank + 人 + for + 事，for 不能丢
I want a burger.（点餐）I'd like a burger.餐厅礼貌用语
No have.No, we don't. / We're out.have 不能直接跟在 no 后面
try the dresstry on the dress试穿必须加 on
20 dollar20 dollars大于1要加 s
He tall than me.He is taller than me.缺be动词和比较级-er
get to thereget therethere/here/home 前不加 to
on saleson sale打折用单数 sale
I don't have brothers and sisters.I don't have brothers or sisters.否定句/疑问句并列用 or 不用 and
🔴 do / be 动词 高频易错
错误正确说明
Do you are a student?Are you a student?be动词句不用do，直接提前be
I very like it.Do you like it?like是动作动词→用do；very不修饰动词
Does she likes tea?Does she like tea?does后动词必须还原
I don't can swim.I can't swim.情态动词can自带否定，不加do
She no like it.She doesn't like it.否定动作动词必须加do/does
Is she like jazz?Does she like jazz?like是动作动词，不能用be提问
🟢 细节提醒
易混项区别
be made of vs fromof = 看得出原材料 / from = 看不出
pay in cash vs by credit cardin + 方式 / by + 工具
cheap vs low pricecheap 修饰物品 / low price 修饰价格
as good as new vs brand new前者≈二手近新 / 后者=真正全新
skillful at vs inat + 具体技能 / in + 领域范围
stall vs shopstall = 集市摊位 / shop = 门店
be in charge of vs be in the charge of前者=负责管理 / 后者=被……管理
start to do vs start doing大部分通用；starting/心理想法→只用 to do
of vs inof 表所属(3 years of experience) / in 表领域(experience in IT)
s后清辅音浊化matchbox /ˈmædʒbɒks/（ch浊化为/dʒ/）；sport /spɔːt/（p浊化为/b/）；stupid /ˈstjuːpɪd/（t浊化为/d/）
🔴 易错点补充(15个文档全汇总)
错误正确说明
suggest to do sthsuggest doing sthsuggest后只能接doing，不能接to do
recommend to do sthrecommend doing sthrecommend后只能接doing，同suggest
go to camp(休闲露营)go camping休闲活动用go doing结构
a blond hairblond hairhair是不可数名词，不能加a
she wearshe wears三单主语，动词必须加s
this position needthis position needs三单主语，动词必须加s
I wish him luckyI wish him luckwish后接名词，不能接形容词
everyone needeveryone needs不定代词视作三单
One of my friends areOne of my friends isone of + 复数 + 单数谓语
go to therego therethere/here/home前不加to
is sunglassesare sunglasses(复数)sunglasses是复数名词
90% discount = 打9折90% discount = 打1折; 10% discount = 打9折discount = 减去的百分比
alway / dollers / credicalways / dollars / credit card拼写易错词汇总
a loaf of breadsa loaf of breadloaf单数，loaves复数;bread不可数
be in the charge of(主动负责)be in charge of(主动) / be in the charge of(被管)有the=被管，无the=主动负责
hasn't friendshas no friends / hasn't got any friendsnot只能否定动词，不能直接否定名词；否定名词用no
🟣 have not / no 用法详解（not vs no）

核心规则：not 是副词，只能否定动词；no 是形容词，直接修饰名词。

错误正确说明
hasn't friendshas no friendsnot不能直接否定名词，用no+名词
hasn't friendshasn't got any friends (英式)haven't got + any + 名词
hasn't friendsdoesn't have any friends (美式)doesn't have + any + 名词
I haven't timeI have no time / I don't have timenot不能直接否定名词time
I haven't moneyI have no money / I don't have moneynot不能直接否定名词money
She hasn't friendsShe has no friends / She doesn't have any friends三单用doesn't have
There aren't problemsThere are no problems / There aren't any problemsthere be否定同样用no或any

📐 三种正确否定have的方式：

① no + 名词 → I have no friends.（最简洁）
② haven't got + any + 名词 → I haven't got any friends.（英式常用）
③ don't/doesn't have + any + 名词 → I don't have any friends.（美式常用）

❌ 绝对不能：

haven't / hasn't + 直接加名词（如 hasn't friends, haven't time）
→ 因为 not 是副词，不能像形容词一样直接修饰名词！

💡 not vs no 对比总结：

词性否定对象例句
not（副词）动词is not / do not / can not
no（形容词）名词no friends / no time / no money

记忆口诀：not配动词，no配名词 — not是副词管动词，no是形容词管名词。

⚠️ MC15 狼来了易错点 MC15
❌ 错误✅ 正确说明
a group of sheepa flock of sheep羊用 flock 不用 group！动物有专属量词：flock羊/鸟、herd牛/鹿、pack狗/狼、school鱼
two sheepstwo sheepsheep 单复数同形！1 sheep / 2 sheep / a flock of sheep
He see villagers runningHe saw villagers runningsee sb doing 可以，但注意时态：故事讲述用过去时 saw/可以
nothing to do but to watchnothing to do but watchnothing to do but 后面接动词原形，不加 to！
The message is being honest.The message is to be honest.表语从句用不定式 to be，不是 being
He lied even telling truth.No one trusts liars even when he tells the truth.even when 引导从句，需要主语+动词
⚠️ 看医生常见错误 健康
❌ 错误✅ 正确说明
I eat medicine.I take medicine.吃药用 take 不用 eat！中文说"吃"药，英文说"服"药
I have headache.I have a headache.headache 可数名词，必须加 a！同理：a fever, a cold, a cough
My head is pain.My head hurts.pain 是名词，hurt 是动词。"我的头疼" → My head hurts.
I have cold.I have a cold. / I caught a cold.感冒必须加 a，且 catch a cold = 感冒（强调传染）
I feel painful.I am in pain. / It is painful.painful 描述事物令人痛苦，不是描述"我痛苦"
Doctor gave me injection.The doctor gave me an injection.injection 可数，需要冠词 an，且 doctor 前需 the
⚠️ 祈使句常见错误 语法
❌ 错误✅ 正确说明
You sit down.Sit down.祈使句省略主语 you！带 You 变成陈述句而非命令
Don't to go.Don't go.Don't 后直接接动词原形，不能加 to！
Let's going.Let's go.Let's 后接动词原形，不是 doing 形式
Not touch.Don't touch. / No touching.否定祈使用 Don't 或 No + doing，不是 Not
Please to sit down.Please sit down.Please 后直接跟原形动词，不加 to
🔴 旅行常见易错 避坑
❌ 中式英语✅ 正确说法原因
I want a burger（点餐）I'd like a burger.I want 太直白，餐厅用 I'd like 礼貌
Can I have menu?Could I have the menu?Could 比 Can 更礼貌，the menu 不能丢 the
I want to live here（酒店）I'd like to stay here.live = 长期居住，stay = 临时住酒店
90% discount = 打9折?10% discount = 打9折discount = 减去的百分比！90% off = 减90%
How to get to station?How do I get to the station?缺少助动词 do，不是 How to 直接开头
get to thereget therethere/here/home 前不加 to
open the lightturn on the light电器/水龙头用 turn on/off，不是 open/close
I very like itI really like it.very 不修饰动词，用 really
My English is poorMy English is basic/limited.poor 太负面了，用 basic 或 limited
Thank your helpThanks for your help.for 不能丢，Thanks = Thank you
Could you have WiFi?Do you have WiFi?询问有无 → do you have，不是 could
give you（递东西）Here you go. / Here you are.give you = 给你（中式），英语用 Here you go
🔴 MC16&22&25&32 新增易错点 MC16&22&25&32
易错点正确用法错误用法
this vs these
指示代词搭配		✅ this capsule (单数)
✅ these capsules (复数)		❌ this capsules
复数名词必须用 these
police 是复数✅ The police are looking into it.❌ The police is looking into it.
forget vs forget about✅ I forgot my umbrella. 忘带伞
✅ Forget about it! 别再想了		❌ 两个混用
forget=遗忘物品；forget about=主观放下
pick up 代词位置✅ pick you up
✅ pick up the clothes		❌ pick up you
代词必须放动副中间
look for 不可拆分✅ look for them❌ look them for
nose vs noisy
听力易混		✅ nose /nəʊz/ 鼻子
✅ noisy /ˈnɔɪzi/ 吵闹的		❌ 听力中混淆两个词
🔴 dessert vs desert 拼写/词义区分 MC8&1
易混项区别
desert 当成甜点dessert = 甜点（两个 s，/dɪˈzɜːt/）
desert = 沙漠（一个 s，/ˈdezət/）
记忆：甜点想吃"两份"(ss) → dessert
拼写混淆 s 个数dessert（甜点，中间是 e）
desert（沙漠，中间也是 e，但只有单 s）
关键看 s 的数量：甜点 ss，沙漠 s
🟡 f/fe 结尾名词变 v 加 -es 规则 MC8&1
❌ 错误✅ 正确说明
lifesliveslife 以 fe 结尾 → 变 v 加 -es
knifesknivesknife → knives
leafsleavesleaf → leaves
直接加 s变 f/fe 为 v 再加 -es规则：以 f/fe 结尾的名词，f/fe → v + es
🔴 live(动词) vs lives(三单/复数) 易混 MC8&1
❌ 混淆✅ 区分说明
He live in the suburbs.He lives in the suburbs.三单 live → lives（加 s）
My live is good.My life is good.（名词"生活"）
My lives（生命复数）		life 名词复数也是 lives，与 live 三单同形，注意词性
lives 当动词原形动词原形是 livelives 是 live 的三单 / life 的复数，不是原形
🔴 because / so 连用（致命）
错误正确说明
Because it rained, so we stayed.Because it rained, we stayed. / It rained, so we stayed.because（原因）与 so（结果）只能用一个
🔴 furniture 不可数（致命）
错误正确说明
a furniture / furnituressome furniture / a piece of furniturefurniture 是不可数名词
🟡 thongs 在澳洲英语
错误正确说明
thongs = 内衣类"丁字裤"thongs = 人字拖（flip-flops）澳式英语用法，= 人字拖
🟡 used to 时态
错误正确说明
I use to... (现在时)I used to... (只有过去)used to 只有过去式
I didn't used to...I didn't use to...否定/疑问里 used 变回 use
🟡 How 问句配对
错误正确说明
How old is the store?（问距离）How far is the store?How big→面积，How tall→高度，How old→年龄，How far→距离
🟡 Sounds 用法
错误正确说明
Sounds a good place.Sounds good. / Sounds like a good place.Sounds + 形容词；Sounds like + 名词
📘 教材常见易错提示
错误正确说明
How much the rent is?How much is the rent?疑问句主语谓语要倒装
get to thereget therethere/here/home 前不加 to
borrow sb sthborrow sth from sbborrow 不直接 + 人 + 物
try the dresstry on the dress试穿必须加 on
20 dollar20 dollars大于1的名词要加 s
I want a burger.（点餐）I'd like a burger.餐厅点餐用 I'd like 更礼貌
arrive the stationarrive at the station / arrive in the city小地点 at / 大地点 in
I very like it.I really like it.very 不修饰动词，用 really
🔴 MC23 生日礼物 · 易错点
错误正确说明
The phone costed me 5000 yuan.The phone cost me 5000 yuan.cost 过去式仍是 cost
I spent 5000 yuan in the phone.I spent 5000 yuan on the phone.spend...on sth
enough specialspecial enough形容词后 enough 后置
money enoughenough money名词前 enough 前置
If I was the woman...If I were the woman...虚拟语气 be 用 were

🗣️ MC29 相亲速配场景句型 MC29
句型中文用法
What are your hobbies / interests?你的爱好是什么？友好开场
What's your favourite food?你最喜欢的食物是什么？安全话题
What kind of movie do you like?你喜欢什么类型的电影？= What's your favourite movie genre?
I think ___ is the best choice for me.我认为……是最适合我的。模板句型
I prefer ___ because ...我更喜欢……因为……模板句型
We both enjoy doing ...我们都喜欢做……共同爱好
___ is more / less + adj. + than ___.……比……更/更不那么……比较级模板
🗣️ MC30 旅行目的地场景句型 MC30
句型中文用法
I'm thinking about where to go on my vacation.我正在考虑假期去哪里。疑问词+不定式
I recommend visiting Buddhist temples.我推荐参观佛寺。recommend doing
You shouldn't miss Mount Fuji.你不应该错过富士山。shouldn't miss
You've got to try sashimi.你一定要尝尝刺身。have got to = must
I hope they are as good as ...我希望它们和……一样好。as + adj + as
I watched street performers dancing on the street.我看见街头艺人在街上表演。watch sb doing
It was really good value for money.它性价比非常高。good value for money
